9a5(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje mi skyod pa/ de ba ni na gshegs pa thams cad kyi mi bzad pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te// byang chub seMs

9a7(rgyud): pa mi skyod pas gsungs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen dpal/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te// 
9a8(rgyud): byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// chos rnams thams cad dngos med cing // chos kyi mtshan nyid rnam par spangs// bdag med chos las kun tu 'byung // byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes bcom
9b1(rgyud): ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen dpal gyis gsungs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag tu med pa 'od zer 'bar ba sgron ma zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang
9b2(rgyud): chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// ma skyes pa'i chos rnams la// ngo bo med te bsgom pa med// nam mkha'i khams su sbyor ba yi// de ltar dngos po rab tu bsgrags// zhes bcom ldan 'das tshe dpag
9b3(rgyud): tu med pas gsungs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa don grub pa gdon mi za ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa/ thams cad zil gyis mi non pa/ rdo rje zhes bya ba'i tinge 'dzin la snyom
9b4(rgyud): par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// chos rnams/ rang bzhin 'od gsal ba// gdod nas dag/ pas na mkha' bzhin// byang chub med cing mngon rtogs med// byang
9b5(rgyud): bachu ba tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshe gas pa grub gdon mi za bas gsungs so// de nas byam pa la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
9b6(rgyud): po rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba'i chos kyi de kho na nyid kyi yi ge thos nas/ ngo mtsha gyur/ rmad du gyur te/ ched du brjod pa 'di med du brjod de/ 
9b7(rgyud): e mya'o sangs rgyas e ma'o chos// chos bshad pa ni ngo mtshar che// yang dag don ni dam pa'i don// byang chub sems la phyag 'tshal lo// bdag med pa'i chos las byung // sangs rgyas byang
9b8(rgyud): chub rdzogs mdzad pa// rnam par mi rtog dmigs su med// byang chub sems la phyag 'tshal lo// kun tu bzang po dam thams cad don// byang chub sems ni rab bskor ba// byang chub spyod pa rdo rje
10a1(rgyud): byang chub sems la phyag 'tshal lo// de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs dag pa// sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje 'dzin// sangs rgyas byang chub rab ston pa// byang chub sems dpa'
10a2(rgyud): la phyag 'tshal mo// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi bsang ba/ 'dus pa las/ byang chub sems kyi le'u ste/ gnyis pa'o// // de na
10a3(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gAsung dang / thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi khro bo'i sprin bkod pa rdo rje zhes bya
10a4(rgyud): ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ rdo rje bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi le'u 'di gsungs so// oM shu n+ye ta dz+nyA na badz+ra swa b+hA bA ang mako ha~M// na mkha'i
10a5(rgyud): dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor bsgom pa ni// 'od zer sprin gyi tshogs chen po// sangs rgyas 'bar ba'i 'od dang mnyam// 'od zer sna lngas kun tu khyab/ 
10a6(rgyud): kun nas yongs su zlum po ste// gzugs kyi lha mo lnga la sogs// 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga yis khyab// mchod pa rnam pa lngas brgyan pa// mdor na de ltar bsgoms nas su// gzugs ni/ 
10a7(rgyud): dbus su bsgom par bya// rnam par snang mdzad phyag rgya che// sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan ma'o// sku gsung thugs ni rdo rje yi/ phyag brgya yang na bsgom par bya// tshogs gnyis dang ni ldan pa mi
10a8(rgyud): mi skyod pa'i rgya mchog dang // rin chen dpal gyi rgya chen dang // tshe dpag med pa'i 'od byed dang // thogs med pa'i rgya chen dang // sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje tsam
10b1(rgyud): in tra ni la'i kha dog 'dra// rab 'bar phyag na rdo rje bsnams// rnam par rtsigs la 'jigs 'jigs ltar// shel dang zla ba'i 'od 'dra ba// thor tshugs gcod pan gyis brgyan pa// rab
10b2(rgyud): 'bar phyag na 'khor lo bsnams// sna tshogs brgyan gyis mdzes par brgyan// 'dzam bu chu bo'i gser 'od 'dra// sangs rgyas sbyin gyis kun tu 'khrigs// de'i phyag na rdo rje che// rtse mo dgu par
10b3(rgyud): rnam par bsgom// mar gid ta'i 'od 'dra ba// rdo rje 'bar bas rnam par brgyan// kun tu 'bar ba'i spyan gyis khyab// phyag na rin chen bsnams par bsgom// pad ma ra ga'i mdog 'dra ba/ 
10b4(rgyud): gtso bo 'dod chags 'bar ba 'dra// rab 'bar phyag na pad ma smras 'dod chags rdo rje can bsgom bya// 'od zer sna lnga'i 'od 'dra zhing // gdon mi za ba'i rdo rje can// zhi ba phyag na ral gri
10b5(rgyud): bsnams// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// de nas bcom ldan 'das de gzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa
10b6(rgyud): thams cad kyi chos kyi dbyings kyi ngo bo nyid rdo rje zhes bya ba'i tingange 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ sku dang / gsung dang / thugs byin gyis rlabs pa'i sngags 'di gsungs so/ oM d+harA d+har
10b7(rgyud): du swa b+ha ba ad ma ko taM// rin chen po kha dog lnga// yungs dkar dang ni 'bru tshod tsam// sna'i rtse mor nan tan bya// rnal 'byor pa yis rtag par bsgom// rin chen brtan par gyur na spro// brtan
10b8(rgyud): par ma gyur yod mi spro// sangs rgyas 'bar ba 'dre ba'i 'od// mchog rab sprin rnams spro bar bya// 'khor lo rdo rje rin chen dang // pad ma ral gri mtshon cha 'dzin// byang chub sems dpa'i sprin chen rgyu/ 
11a1(rgyud): spro ba'i bdag nyid can gyis s+ho// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor bri bar bya// gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// 'khor lo dkyil 'khor
11a2(rgyud): bsgom par bya// pad ma'i dkyil 'khor 'dra bar ni// zlas pa snyoms pas sgom par bya// rin chen dkyil 'khor 'dri bar ni// rin chen bsgom pas sgom par bya// sbyor ba'i dkyil 'khor las
11a3(rgyud): byung ba// nomakha' 'dra bar bri bar bya// 'di dag sangs rgyas rab kyi mchog/ sku gsung thugs ni bsgom pa yis// dkyil 'khor rdo rje las byung ba// thams cad mkhyen pa'i tshul 'thob pa'o// 
11a4(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang // gsung dang thugs/ kyi/ gsang ba 'dus pa las/ rdo rje bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi le'u ste/ gsum pa'o// 
11a5(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yang 'dus nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi bdag po la bstod
11a6(rgyud): pa'i rgyal po 'dis gsol bya gdab po// de bzhin gshegs pa kun zhi ba// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gnas// chos kun bdug med pa yi mchog/ dkyil 'khor dam pa bshad du gsol// 
11a7(rgyud): mtshan rnams thams cad yongs su rdzogs// mtshan min thams cad yang dag spangs// kun tu bzang po sku'i mchog/ dkyil 'khor dam pa bshad du gsol// zhi ba'i 'od ni mchog las
11a8(rgyud): khyung // ye shes spyod pa rnam sbyong ba// kun du bzang po gsung gi mchog/ dkyil 'khor dam pa bshad du gsol// sems can kun gyi sems chen po// rang bzhin dag cing dri ma med/ 
11b1(rgyud): kun bzang thugs mchog kha lo bsgyur// dkyil 'khor dam pa bshad du gsol// de nas ston pa rdo rje 'dzin// 'jig rten gsum pa khams gsum pa// 'jig rten gsum mchog rdo rje gtso/ 
11b2(rgyud): 'jig rten gsum mchog ston pa pos// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gnas// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi thugs// dkyil 'khor dkyil 'khor rab 'dra ba// dkyil 'khor rab tu nyams dga'
11b3(rgyud): bshad// de nas thugs kyi dkyil 'khor mchog/ thugs kyi rdo rje rab 'dra ba// sku dang gsung dang thugs rnams kyis// dkyil 'khor rab tu bshad par bya// lus ngag sems ni bsgoms pa yis2
11b4(rgyud): shes rab can gyis thig gdab pa// thig skud gsar pa legs de bka' ba// tshad ma rab tu mdzes pa yis/ thugs kyi dkyil 'khor dam pa de// khru ni bcu gnyis tshad du bya// ngos bzhi
11b5(rgyud): dang ni grwa bzhir ldan// sgo bzhi pa ni rab tu brtag/ de'i dbus su 'khor lo ni// rab tu zlum por bri bar bya// de nas lam gyi cho ga ni// mthong bas phyag rgya dgod par bya// de dbus
11b6(rgyud): rdo rje bri ba ni// in tA ni la'i kha dog 'dra// 'bar ba chen po'i rtse lnga pa// 'jigs pa dag kyang rab 'jigs byed// 'khor lo chen po shar phyogs su// rdo rje 'bar bas rnam par brgyan// rin chen chen
11b7(rgyud): po lnga phyogs su// 'od zer mang po rab tu 'khrigs// pad+ma ma chen po nub phyogs su// padad+ma ma rA gA'i kha dog 'dra// ral gri chen po byang phyogs su// 'od zer mang po rab tu 'khrug/ dbus su sbyin
11b8(rgyud): dang 'dra ba'i 'od// spyan ni shar gyi grwa ru gzigs// ma ma ki ni rigs byung ba'i// rdo rje de bzhin lho phyogs su// pad ma kha phye sdong bur bcas// nub phyogs su ni bri bar bya// ud pal mdzes pa
13a1(rgyud): byang phyogs su// mthing ka sprin dang 'dra ba bri// tho ba 'bar ba 'od gsal ba// shar phyogs 'bar sogs 'od bzang ba// be con lho'i phyogs su bri// pad ma 'bar ba 'od 'byed pa
13a2(rgyud): nub kyi phyogs su bri bar bya// rdo rje 'khyil ba rdo rje can// byang gi phyogs su bri bar bya// thugs kyi dkyil 'khor dam pa de// yongs su gsal bar shes par byas na// lus dang ngag sems mchod pa yis
13a3(rgyud): nan tan du ni mchod par bya// bud med rab tu mdangs bzang ba// lo grangs bcu drug lon pa ni// dri dang phreng brgyan dang ni// yon tan skye regs ma ma kIr// shes rab can gyi byin rlabs la// de'i
13a4(rgyud): dbus su mnyes par bya// sangs rgyas zhi ba'i gnas spros pas// na mkha' dbyings ni rab tu brgyan// gshang lci khro ba khrag la sogs// lha rnams la ni dbul bar bya// de ltar
13a5(rgyud): byas na sangs rgyas dang // byang chub sems dpa' grags chen rnams// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba 'dus pa las/ de bzhin gshegs pa
13a6(rgyud): thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor gyi le'u ste/ bani pa'o// / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa ni// kun gyi sku dang gsung thugs kyi// rdo rje 'chang ba'i rgyal po ni// gnas kyi dpung
13a7(rgyud): phyug kun mchog gis// spyod pa kun mchog gis rjes kyi don// stong pa'i mtshan nyid bka' stsal pa// rnam par tshig don las byung // 'dod rmugs zhe sdang grang mug rigs// theg pa'i mchog
13a8(rgyud): ni bla na med// dngos gru bor ba mchog 'grub par byed// rigs ngan smyig ma mkhan la sogs// gsod don don gnyer sems pa rnams// theg chen bran med pa yi// theg mchog 'di las
13b1(rgyud): 'grub par 'gyur// sems can 'tshams med la sogs pa'i// sdig pa chen po byed pa yang // rdo rje theg pa rgya mtsho der/ theg pa mchog ni 'di las 'grub// snying nas slob dpon smod pa dag
13b2(rgyud): sgrubs kyang 'grub par yong mi 'gyur// srog gcod pa'i sems can gang // brdzun du sbrul dga' ba dang // gzhan gyi nor la chags pa dang // rtag tu 'dod pa spyod gang dang // gtsang gci zas
13b3(rgyud): su za ba ste// de dag bsgrub pa'i snod du gyur// ma dang sring mo bu mo la// 'dod pa las ni nyes byas na// theg pa mchog gi chos nyid kyi// dngos grub rgya chen des thob po// sangs rgyas gtso
13b4(rgyud): be'i yum drag la// rnam par mi rtog blo can gyis// nyes par rna ra byas kyang mi gos te// de ni sangs rgyas du 'grub par 'gyur// de nas sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba la sogs
13b5(rgyud): pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams ngo mtshar du gyur te/ rmad du gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po ci'i slad du/ de bzhin
13b6(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi nang du 'di lta bu'i tshig ngan pa gsung zhes gsol to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba la sogs pa'i byang chub sems
13b7(rgyud): dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi tshig gsan nas/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu rnams thong / de skad ma zer cig/ snying po ye shes can
13b8(rgyud): rnams kyi// sangs rgyas chos nyid dag pa 'di// snying po chos kyi don las byung // byang chub spyod pa'i gnas 'di yin// de nas yang brjod kyis mi lang ba'i yang brjod kyis mi lang ba'i
14a1(rgyud): sangs rgyas kyi ning phra rab la sogs pa'i rdul phra mo skyed kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnams skrag nas rgyal bar gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis
14a2(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' de dag rgyal bar gyur pa gzigs nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs kyi rdo rje bdag po la/ 'di skad ces gsol to// 
14a3(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'di dag srung bar gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rjes de bzhin gshegs pa nam
14a4(rgyud): mkha' dang mnyam pa gnyis su med pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin// la snyoms par bzhugs so// snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
14a5(rgyud): kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i bdag nyid po'i 'od kyis reg pa tsam gyis/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag rang gi bstan la gnas par gyur to// de nas de
14a6(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ngo mtshar du gyur/ rmad du gyur/ dges pas khyab par gyur nas/ chos kyi dbyings 'di skad ces gsungs so// e ma'o chos e ma'o chos e mra'o chos kyi don ma
14a7(rgyud): byung ba// chos don dag pa bdug med pa// rdo rje rgyu la la phyag 'tshal 'dud// sku dang gsung thugs rab tu dgra/ na mkha' dang ni mnyam nyid gnas// rnam par mi 'gyur snang ba med// rdo rje sku la
14a8(rgyud): phyag 'tshal 'dud// thugs ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i gtso// dus gsum dag pa'i lam du byung // na mkha' chen po dbyings gyur pa// na mkha'i lam la phyag 'tshal 'dud// nam mkha'i sku las
14b1(rgyud): yang dag 'byung // na mkha'i lam la gnas pa po// na mkha'i thugs de chos kyi mchog/ spyod pa'i gnas la phyag 'tshal lo// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs kyi
14b2(rgyud): gsang ba 'dus pa sras/ kun gyi spyod pa'i mchog gi le'u ste/ lnga pa'o// / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa mi spyod pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsu
14b3(rgyud): dang thugs kyi gsang ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ thugs byin gyis brlab pa'i sngags 'di gsungs so// oM sarba ta thA g+ha ta tsit+ta badz+ra sa b+ha ba ad ma kaM ha~M/ 
14b4(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje rnam parasnang mdzad/ rdul dang bral ba'i gnas/ zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ sku byin gyi brlob
14b5(rgyud): pa'i sngags 'di gsung so// oM sarba ta thA g+hA ta ka ya badz+ra swa b+hA ba ad mako hA// de nas de bzhin ga she gas la tshe dpag med mnyam pa nyid gnas pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting
14b6(rgyud): 'dzin sa snyoms par zhugs te/ gsung byin gyis brlab pa'i sngags 'di gsungs so// oM sarba thA g+ha ta wab badz+ra sa b+ha ba ang mgo ha~M// rdo rje gsum po de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsang
14b7(rgyud): gnas ni gnas kyis rnam par bsgom par bya// sngags kyis mtshan gyis shin tu mtshan byas la// mchog ra ba 'di yis bsgrub pa nyid du bya// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
14b8(rgyud): dkon dpal ye shes sgron ma rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ sngags 'di gsungs so// oM sarba ta thA g+ha ta a nu ra ga na badz+ra sap+pa be ad pra ko haM// de nas bcom
15a1(rgyud): galdan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa grub pa rdo rje gdon mi za ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ sngags 'di gsungs so// oM sarba ta thA g+hA ta pU dza badz+ra swa b+hA ba
15a2(rgyud): ad mo ko haM// rtag tu 'dod pa'i yon lngas// sangs rgyas tshul bzhin mchod par bya// mchod pa rnam pa lnga rnams kyis// myur du sangs rgyas nyid thob 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
15a3(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi bdag po rdo rje 'chang bas gsungs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs
15a4(rgyud): kyi bdag po rdo rje 'dzin gyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngags kyi gsang ba 'di gsungs so// sngags la dmigs pa'i lus dang ni// ngag dang yid kyis skul nas su/ 
15a5(rgyud): yid ni dga' nas ning mgu nas su// dngos grub rab mchog sgrub par bya// sems la dmigs bdag med pas// ngag dang lus kyang rnam par bsgom// na mkha' bzhin du mnyam
15a6(rgyud): pa'i gnas// sbyor ba rnam gsum sgrub par bya// lus dang ngag dang sems dmigs na// ngo bo nyid ni dmigs su myed// sngags kyis lus su sbyor blta// byang chub med cing bsgom pa med// sku
15a7(rgyud): gsung thugs kyi mtsho nyid du// 'di ni mdor ni rnam spyad na// sngags kyis brtags pa'i ting nge 'dzin// byang chub sbyor ba sgom par bya// de nas dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzin// de bzhin gshegs pa kun
15a8(rgyud): gyis mchod// sangs rgyas kun mchog kun mkhyen gyi// sgom pa'i mchog ni bka' stsal to// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor sgom par bya// sangs rgyas gzugs ni
15b1(rgyud): ra snyosas nus/ ma mo'i sbyor bkun cu cug/ sna na mor srungs dkar bsam// 'gro dang ma 'gro srungs da sa// ye shes gnas ni mas dka' ba// gsang ba'i mi shes kyis rtags sngon
15b2(rgyud): namakha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor sgom par bya// sangs rgyas sku'i gnas snyoms te// de'i steng na gnas bzhag go// hUM na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par/ 
15b3(rgyud): gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor sgom par bya// spyan gyi tshul tu sbyor ba la// rdo rje pad ma rnam par bsgom// namakha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// rin chen dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// dang po'i skye
15b4(rgyud): ba nan tan gyis// de'i steng du yongs bsgom par// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// pad ma'i/ dkyil 'khor sgom par bya// gsung gi rdo rje tshul sbyor bas// 'dod chags
15b5(rgyud): rdo rje can bsgom bya// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus par// 'od kyi dkyil 'khor sgom par bya// sangs rgyas tshul ni zhi ba sgo// 'khor dang khyad par dag tu spro// ud pas 'bring ka'i
15b6(rgyud): mdog 'dra ba// rtse mo lnga pa khyad par du// nas kyi 'bru tsam nan tan gyis// sna'i rtse mor rnam par bsnam// tsa na ka'i 'bru tsam la// 'dab ma brgyad pa ge sor bcas// sna'i rtse mor 'di shes te/ 
15b7(rgyud): sgoms pas byang chub gzhol bar 'gyur// 'khor lo la sogs khyad par du// sku gsung bsgom pa de ni rtag par bya// dngos grub thams cad yon tan gnas// nyams dga' byang chub gnas 'grub
15b8(rgyud): 'gyur// sangs rgyas byang chub gnas rnams ni// de ru mdor na spro bar bya// sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan ma yis// chos kyi tshig rnams rab tu brjod// de nas dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzin// de nyid don tu ston pagro// 
16a1(rgyud): spyod pa kun mchog legs dag pa// gsang sngags dam pa bka' stsal to// gzugs dang sgra dang ror ldan pa// shes rab can gyis zla drug bsgom// gsang ba'i de nyid mchod chen gyis// legs
16a2(rgyud): par mchod sgom par bya// dngos grub 'bras bu 'dod pa yis// zas su gshang lci zos nas ni// sangs rgyas byang chub skyon med pa// yang dag bla med 'grub par 'gyur// zas su sha rnams za ba dang / 
16a3(rgyud): sha chen dag ni rab brtags nas// sku gsung thugs dang gsang ba yi// dngos grub thams cad 'grub par 'gyur// glang po'i sha dang rta'i sha// de bzhin dam khyi'i sha// zas kyi phyir ni bza' bar bya// 
16a4(rgyud): zas gzhan dag ni ma zos na// byang chub sems dpa' tho can dang // sangs rgyas rnams ni mnyes par 'gyur// 'di lta bu'i sbyor ba yis// myur du sangs rgyas nyid 'gyur// 'dod khams
16a5(rgyud): dbang phyug 'jig rten na// go 'phangs las ni byed par 'gyur// tsa bo gzi can spobs dang ldan// mdangs bzang mthong na yid du 'ong // mthong ba tsam gyis skul ba yis// 'jig rten 'di
16a6(rgyud): dag dbang du gyur// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// gsang ba'i byang chub dam pa ste// yang dge sngags kyi gsang ba 'di// lus ngag sems las 'da' ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
16a7(rgyud): sku dang // gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba 'dus pa las/ sku dang thugs byin gyi brlab pa'i le'u ste/ drug pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi skur
16a8(rgyud): gsung dang / thugs kyi bdapo pos/ dam tshig po'i 'di de kho na nyid sngags spyod pa'i mchog mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i le'u 'di gsungs so// 'dod pa'i longs spyod thams cad la// rjes
16b1(rgyud): 'dod par sten na ni// 'dis bu'i sbyor ba yis// sangs rgyas myur du thob par 'gyur// 'dod pa'i yang spyong thams cad ni// ji ltar 'dod pa sten byas te// rang gi lha'i sbyor ba yis// bdag dang gnan
16b2(rgyud): ma mchod par bya// dka' thub sdom pa mi bzad pas// snron kyang 'grub par mi 'gyur gyi// 'dod pa'i longs spyod thams cad la// spen na byur du 'grub par 'gyur// spongs po za zhing mi bzlas te/ 
16b3(rgyud): slong la'ang dga' bar bya'o// 'dod pa kun la long spyod cing // sngags kyi yan lag ma nyams zla// lus dang ngag dang sems rnams ni// bde bar gnas nas byang chub thob// gzhan du dus min 'chi ba dang / 
16b4(rgyud): dmyal bar nges par bsreg par 'gyur// sangs rgyus byang chub sems dpa' dang // sngags kyi spyod pa'i mchog spyod rnams// chos mchog mi g.yo mnyes pa yang // 'dod pa thams
16b5(rgyud): cod sten pas so// chags chen ye shes 'dod pa yis// rtag tu 'dod yon lnga rnams sten// byang chub nyi ma tshogs par bya// gzugs la rnam gsum shes byas nas// mchod
16b6(rgyud): pa med pas mchod par bya// de nyid bcom ldan 'das sna tshogs// sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad bzhi// sgra la rnam gsum shes byas nas// lha rnams la ni dbul bar bya// de nyid bcom ldan sna
16b7(rgyud): tshogs pa// sangs rgyas rin chen 'byung ldan gtso// dri la rnam gsum shes byas nas// sangs rgyas tshogs dbul bar bya// de nyid bcom ldan sna tshogs pa// 'dod chagos chos kyi 'byung gnas
16b8(rgyud): gtso// rol rnam gsum shes byas nas// lha rnams la ni dbul bar bya// de nyid sangs rgyas sna tshogs pa// sangs rgyas thogs med rdo rje 'dzin// reg la rnam gsum shes byas nas// bdag gi rigs la
17a1(rgyud): dbul bar bya// de nyid bcom ldan rdo rje 'dzin// mi skyod pa'i tshul mnyes pa// gzugs sgra ro la stegs pa la// rtag tu sems ni sbyar bar bya// 'di de sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// gsang ba'i snying po
17a2(rgyud): bsdus pa'o// gzugs sgra dri sngogs sngags pa yi// lha nyid du ni rnam par bsgom// yang na de la bsgom pa ni// rigs kyi tshul du rnam par bsgom// sangs rgyas rjes su dran par sbyor// khro bo rjes su dran sgom pa/ 
17a3(rgyud): lha ni rjes su dran pa sbyor// bsgoms na byang chub 'thob par 'gyur// bud med gzugs bzang mdangs ldan pa// lo grangs bcu drug lon pa la// byin gyis rlabs kyis gnas gsum du// dben par mchod pa
17a4(rgyud): rab tu rtsam// de bzhin gshegs pa'i btsun mo mchog/ spyan la sogs par bsgom par bya// dbang po gnyis ni mnyam sbyar bas// sangs rgyas dngos grub thob par 'gyur// yi ge hUM dang
17a5(rgyud): oM dag kyang // phaT kyang rab tu bsgom par bya// 'od zer rnam lngas khyab pa yis// pad ma rdo rje bsgom par bya// 'bar bcos zla 'od bzhin du dkar// yid du 'ong ba sbyin par bya// sangs
17a6(rgyud): rgyas rjes dran sbyor la sogs// byang chub 'dod pas bsgom par bya// de la sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na// b+ha ga la ni ling ga gzhag/ sangs rgyas rjes dran mo gzugs ni bsgom par bya// 
17a7(rgyud): ba sku rnams kyi bu gnas pa// mkhas pas chos kyi sprin rnams spro// de la rdo rjes rjes su dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na// b+ha ga la ni ling ga gzhag/ rdo rje se tshe'idapa' rnam par sgom// ba sku rnams kyi bu ga gnas// 
17a8(rgyud): rdo rje sgron rnams spro bar bya// de la rigs rjes su dran pa ni ji ltar bsgom zhe na/ b+ha ga sa ni ling ga gzhag/ sangs rgyas gzugs ni rab tu bsgom// ba spu rnams kyi bu ga gnas// mkhas pas rigs
17b1(rgyud): kyi sprin rnams spro// de la khro ba rjes su dran pa ji ltar sgrom zhe na// b+ha ga le ni ling ga gzhag/ khro bo'i dpa' bo rab tu sgom// ba spu rnams kyi bu gnas// mkhas pas pas khre bo'i sprin rnams spro// de sa
17b2(rgyud): dam tshig rjes su dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhen// bdag gi rdo rje pad mar ldan// dbang po gnyis ni mnyam sbyor te// rang gi khu ba'i thigs pa yis// sangs rgyas rdo rje sems dpa' mchod// de la dkyil 'khor
17b3(rgyud): rjes su dran pa ji lhur bsgom zhe na/ dbang po gnyis ni mnyam bzhag ste// mkhas pas rang gi khu ba bdag/ rnal 'byor pas ni rtag tu byung // dkyil 'khor dkyil 'khor tshul du bya// de sngar su rjes su dran
17b4(rgyud): pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na// sangs rgyas kun gyi sku gang yin// phung po lnga yis rab tu rgyas// sangs rgyas sku'i rang bzhin gyis// bdag kyang de dang 'ang gyur cig/ de la gsung rjes su dran pa ji ltar sgom zhe na/ 
17b5(rgyud): rdo rje chos kyi gsung gang yin// gsung des nges tshig phun sum// tshogs// bdag gi tshig kyang de 'dra ste// chos 'dzin pa dang 'dra gyur cig/ de la thugs rjes su dran pa ji ltar sgom zhe na/ 
17b6(rgyud): gsang ba'i bdag po blo ldan pa// kun tu bzang po'i thugs gang yin// rdo rje 'dzin pa lta bu ste// bdag kyang de dang 'dra gyur cig/ de la sems can rjes su dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na/ sems can kun gyi
17b7(rgyud): sems gang yin// sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi mtshan// de ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// mkhas dang mtshungs par sbyong gyur cig/ de la sngags thams cad kyi gzugs dang // sku dang gsung dang / thugs rjes
17b8(rgyud): su dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na/ sngags kyi rdo rje'i sku gang yin// gsung gi sku yang rnam bsgom pa// bdag kyang rtag tu de 'dra bar// sngags 'dzin pa dang mnyam gyur cig/ de la dam tshig rjes su dran pa ji ltar
18a1(rgyud): bsgom zhe na/ khu ba byung ste chog bzhin// dbus su 'dod pas btung bar bya// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshogs gsang na// dngos grub rab tu 'ong bar 'gyur// de la shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin
18a2(rgyud): pa'i dam tshig rjes su dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na// rang bzhin gyis ni 'od gsal ba// thams cad ma skyes zag pa med// byang chub med cing mngon rtogs med// khams gsum med dbyung ba med// de la
18a3(rgyud): ma skyes pa rjes su dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na// thams cad rang bzhin 'od gsal ba// mtshan med mi 'gyur na mkha' bzhin// gnyis med gnyis su med min zhing // shin du dri med na mkha' bzhin// de la
18a4(rgyud): zhe sdang gi rigs la sogs pa mchod pa rjes su dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na// bud med sems ni rab brtan pa// lo grangs bcu gnyis lon rnyed la// rigs kyi sbyor bas rab sgoms te// bang gi
18a5(rgyud): khu bas mchod par bya// 'dis ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku// rdo rje 'dzin pa'i thugs dang ni// chos 'dzin mchog gi gsung dag dang // tshe 'di nyid la thob par 'gyur// sku dang gsung nga
18a6(rgyud): thugs kyang 'grub// gang gang phra mor bshad pa'i rnams// rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms te// zlas pa tsam gyis de 'grub 'gyur// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gas
18a7(rgyud): 'dus pa las/ sngags kyi spyod pa'i mchog gi le'u ste// / bdun pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje dkon mchog dpas gyis/ bcom ldan 'das de
18a8(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po dbang phyug dam pa rdo rje 'dzin chen po la bstod pa 'dis gsol ba btab po// rdo rje sems dpa' theg pa che// na mkha'i spyod pa rnam sbyong ba// kun du bzang po sbyong / 
18b1(rgyud): pa'i mchog/ rgyal mchog mchod pa bshad du gsol// 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug che// rdo rje theg pa rab ston pa// na mkha'i dbyings dang mtshungs pa'i mchog/ rgyal ba zhi mchod pa bshad du gsol/ 
18b2(rgyud): thar pa'i lam ni rab ston pa// theg pa gsum gyi lam la gnas// sangs rgyas skal mchog dag pa'i bdag/ mi mchog mchod pa bshad du gsol// byang chub sems ni rgyas pa'i spyan// chos kyi 'khor lo
18b3(rgyud): rab skor ba// sku dang thagasung dang thugs ni shin tu dag/ phyag 'tshas rdo rje theg pa la'o// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// thams cad namakha'i mi 'gyur tshe// thams cad dbang sror nyid kyi don// kun dbang / 
18b4(rgyud): rdo rje rin chen 'dzin// de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod pa mchog/ rdo rje mi phyed gsum gnas pa// sku dang gsung dang thugs la sgras mchog/ rgyas pa 'byung bar 'gyur bar bshad/ na
18b5(rgyud): rlungs gnon nu mig yangs dang // gzugs bzangs pa no// pas brgyan pa no// lo grangs nyi shu lnga lon rnyed// byol so las kyang rab tu brtag/ sa phyogs gtsang zhing rnam dben pa 'an
18b6(rgyud): 'di skyes zhing na pa'i gnas rnams su// gshang kyi num sogs pa byug pa'o// / rgyas pan chod phyir rtag par rab tu bya// nus ring bus par sbyi n+yag mtha'i bang // dog shes pas 'ang na nang pa'i bad
18b7(rgyud): skye ba byed pa gsang brgyal pa'i sras// rigs snga rnams ni dgod par rab tu bya// nA mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// ye shes rgyam tshe sbom par bya// bdag nyid zla ba'i dbus gnas par// mkhas pa
18b8(rgyud): snying khor rnam par bya// zhi ba rdo rje 'dzin 'dod na// bcus pa dag kyang rab tu bya// rin cen sngo bzhi'i mchod rten pa// 'od zer phreng bas rnam par brgyan// ye zhes rgya mo dus gzul rtse// gnas de yin par/ 
20a1(rgyud): rnam par bsam// bdag gi baspu'i bu gnas// mkhas pas mchod pa'i sprin rnams sgro// mkhas pas ud pa la dag dang // pad ma rnam pa lnga shes bya// dza ti rnam gsum shes byas nas// lha rnams la yang
20a2(rgyud): dbul bar bya// me tog gar gi kar dang // ma mi ka dang yu tika/ me tog ka ra bir bsam// mchid pa thams cad rab tu brtag/ dpag tshad brgya'i khyon tsam la// gru ba ni shin du mdzes pa la// 'khor lo dkyil lalo
20a3(rgyud): bsgom bya la// rnam par rtag pas rtag par ni// rigs rnams rab tu dgod par bya// de bzhin gshegs pa pad mo rdo rje dang // ral gri ud mkhas pas bsgom// dpag tshad bye ba'i khyon tsam la// gru ba ni shin tu mdzes pa
20a4(rgyud): yis// mchod rten rin chen sna bzhi la// gsal zhing rang bzhin dri ma med// rigs rnams thams cad mchod pa'i phyir// shes rab da can gyi gnas su bsgom// 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga rnams kyis// de la mchod
20a5(rgyud): pargya mtsho rtsam// rin chen na bza' la sogs pas// byang chub 'dod pas rtag tu mchod// mchod pa rnam lnga'i mchog rnams kyis// rtag tu lha rnams brnyes par bya// rin chen 'byung gnas na chung
20a6(rgyud): mchog/ rin chen sna tshogs mchog gis brgyan// bsgrub chen rab tu 'grub pa'i phyir// ma sangs rgyas kun la dbul bar bya// zhing 'dir rin chen sna bdun gyis// mkhas pa dag gis yongs bkang la// dngos
20a7(rgyud): grub 'dod par sbyin pa'i phyir// nyin re shes rab can gyis dbul// bdag po phyag rgyas mnyam bzhag la// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dbus dag tu// 'dod chags bro can sangs rgyas la// dngos grub
20a8(rgyud): 'dod par sbyin po'i phyir// reg pa'i sbyor ba dbul bar bya// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// dkyil 'khor bkod pa bsgom par bya// de bzhin gshegs pa bdag gi sus// bla ma gshang dang
20b1(rgyud): lci bas mchod// bzhin bzangs shin tu mdzes pa yis// na rlung rgal ba mchog ldan pa// byin gyis brlabs kyis gnas bsams te/ sangs rgyas mchod pa rab tu brtag/ mig bzangs ldan pa'i blo ldan
20b2(rgyud): bas// khub rdzangs nas bza' bar bya// 'di ni sngags rnams thams cad kyis// sku gsung thugs kyi mchod pa ste// ye shes rdo rje can gyis gsung // sngags rnams dngos grub byed par gsungs// de lazhin
20b3(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba/ gsang ba 'dres pa las/ gcang gci'i dam tshig gi le'u ste/ brgyad pa'o// / de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin
20b4(rgyud): thams cad na mkha' mi 'gyur tshe// thams cad dbang skur spyod pa'i mchog/ dbang phyug dam pa kun don gyi// sku gsung thugs kyi longs spyod pa// rdo rje mi phyed gsum dkyil 'khor// sangs rgyas ye shes
20b5(rgyud): can gyis gsang // nyams dga' mchog ni rab tu bshad// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// sangs rgyas dkyis 'khor bsgom par bya// rdo rje mi skyod rab bsgoms nas// lag tu rdo rje/ 
20b6(rgyud): bsgom par bya// 'od 'phro mang po 'bar ba dang // 'od zer sna sngas rab tu gang // dus gsum pa'i sangs rgyas rnams// snyoms nas rdo rje phye mar brlag/ sku gsung thugs kyi long spyod ni// rdo rje cher
20b7(rgyud): grags med par gyur pa// bsam gtan mchog de bsgoms na ni// thugs kyi dngos grub thob par 'gyur// rdo rje gsang ba 'di lta bus// sems can thams cad gsang na ni// mi skyod sangs rgyas zhing dag tu
20b8(rgyud): rgyal ba'i sras su skye bar 'gyur// 'di ni zhe sdang gi rigs kyi dam tshig gi de kho na nyid sde/ rigs thams cad kyi ma rgya mtsho yin par shes par bya'o// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// ye shes thar pa rab sgrub pa/ 
21a1(rgyud): ngo bo nyid dag gos pa med// byang chub spyod pa rab ston pas// sangs rgyas byang chub sgrub pa yis// yang dag dam tshig bka' stsal to// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// 'khor lo
21a2(rgyud): dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// rnam par snang mdzad rab bsgoms te// sangs rgyas thams cad rnam par sgom// rin chen kun gyi sbyor ba yis// rdo rje gzugs ni rab tu brtag/ nor rnams cad phrogs na su// 
21a3(rgyud): rdo rje gsum tu rnams bsgoms na// nor gyi rgya mtsho gang ba yi// yid bzhin nor bu 'dra bar 'gyur// rdo rje gsum du rnam par bsgoms sangs rgyas kun gyi sgras rnams dang // thub pa'i skyes bu mchog tu 'gyur// 
21a4(rgyud): 'di ni rigs kyi rgya mtsho thams cad las// gti mug gi rig kyi dam tshig yang dag pa nyid du shes par bya'o// de nas rgyal ba rdo rje 'dzin// 'dod chags thar pa rab sgrub par// gsang ba dam pa da mi
21a5(rgyud): med pa'i// dkyil 'khor rab tu bka' stsal to// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// pad ma'i dkyim 'khor bsgom par bya// dpag med chos ni rab bsgoms te// sangs rgyas
21a6(rgyud): rnams kyis thams cad gang // bud med mar bur sbyar ba ni// dam tshig bzhi'i sbyor ba yis// thams cad bana'i de ru bsgom par bya// 'di ni rdo rje'i tshul mchog go/ dbang po gnyis ni rab sbyor bas// de dag
21a7(rgyud): thams cad nye bar spyad// 'di ni rdo rje thams cad kyis// mi byed sku gsum bsgom pa'o// 'di ni 'dod chags kyis yang dag pa'i dam tshig sde// sngags rnams kyis bsgom par bya'o// de nas rgyas po rdo rje 'dzin/ 
21a8(rgyud): rdo rje sngags kyis don grub pa// bdag med me shes las byung // gsung ni 'di skad bka' stsal to// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// rdo rje thogs med rnaM
21b1(rgyud): bsgoms te// sangs rgyas thams cad bsgom par bya// thams cad gzugs su rnams sgoms te// rdo rje tshig gi brdzun smras pas// rgyas pa kun gyi gnas rnams dang // rgyal ba thams cad smra bar bya// 'di ni
21b2(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// na mkha'i gsung ste dri med pa// ye shes blo can kun gyi gsong // sngags kyi dngos grub thob par bshad// 'di ni dam tshig dgug pa'i rigs kyi dam tshig gi de kho na nyid do// don gyi
21b3(rgyud): lta ba bzhin du spro bar bya'o// de nas rgyal ba rdo rje 'dzin// rdo rje mi phyed gsum rgyal gnas// rdo rje dngos grub rab ston pa// gsung ni 'di skad bka' stsal te// ni mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// dam tshig
21b4(rgyud): dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// dkon mchog dpal ni rab bsgoms te// gzugs rnams kun gyis 'di dag gang / rtsub pa'i ngag la sogs pa ni// sten na ye shes thob par 'gyur// bcom
21b5(rgyud): ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje bkod pas de skad ces bka' stsal to// de nas yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig rdo rje dpal la sogs pa'i byang chub
21b6(rgyud): sems dpa' chen po rnams ngo mtshar du gyur cing // rmad du gyur nas/ rdo rje'i tshig 'di smras so// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po khams gsum las 'das shing / 'jig
21b7(rgyud): rten las 'das pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi nang du 'di lta bu'i yang dag pa ma mchis par yin pa'i tshig gi lam rdo rje'i tshig ci'i slad du gsung / de nas
21b8(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis/ brjod kyis mi lang ba'i yang brjod kyis mi lang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi ri rab kyi rdul phra rab mo snyed kyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig
22a1(rgyud): rdo rje dpal la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu dman pa'i 'du shes dang / smad pa'i 'du shes 'di lta bu ma bskyed cig/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 
22a2(rgyud): rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ sngags kyi spyod pa ni spyod pa'i mchog go// 'di lta ste/ sngags kyi spyod pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod pa'o// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na na mkha' ni chos thams cad kyi rjes su
22a3(rgyud): song ba ste/ chos thams cad kyang na mkha'i ngang du gtogs pa'o// chos de dag thams cad kyang 'dod pa'i khams na mi gnas// gzugs kyi khams na mi gnas/ gzugs med pa'i khams na mi gnas
22a4(rgyud): 'byung ba chen po bzhi la yang mi gnas so// rigs kyi bu chos thams cad kyang de ltar shes par bya'o// de bzhin gshegs pa rnams ni don gyi dbang 'di lta bu mkhyen cing / sems can
22a5(rgyud): rnams kyi bsam pa mkhyen nas/ chos 'chad par mdzad rda/ rigs kyi bu na mkha'i tshig de ltar brjod pas/ de banani/ gshegs pa'i dam tshig de dag rjes su rig par bya'o// rigs kyi bu'
22a6(rgyud): lnga ste dper na/ rtsub shing dang / rtsub stan dang / mi'i lag pa spyod pa'i rkyen gyis du bu myur du 'byung zhing / me 'byung bar 'gyur mod kyi/ me de yang gtsub shing la mi gnas/ gtsu bstan lnga yang mi gan+d+ha
22a7(rgyud): mi'i lag bskyod pa la yang mi gnas// rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje dam tshig 'gro ba dang / 'ong ba la sogs pas rjes su rig par bya'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag
22a8(rgyud): mtshar du gyur/ rmad du gyur nas/ ngam zhig ming gdangs nas/ tshig 'di skad ces smraso// rmad 'byung chen po'i chos rnams ni// na mkha' dang ni mtshungs po dang // rnam par mi rtog dag pa la// kun rdzob
22b1(rgyud): du yang bshad par mtshar// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa las/ don dam pa'i dag pa de kho na nyid kyi don gyi dam tshig gi le'u ste/ 
22b2(rgyud): dgu pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yang 'dus te/ bcom ldan 'das dam tshig chen po rdo rje kho na nyid mngon par rdzogs par byang chub bsku dang / gsung
22b3(rgyud): dang thugs dang / de bzhin gshegs pa la phyag 'tshal te/ 'di skad ces gsom to// de nyid sngags skyong kun bsdus pa// sku dang gsung dang thugs gsapa skyugs// dngos grub chen po drug kyi 'chog
22b4(rgyud): yang dgra bcom ldan bshad du gsol// de nas rgyal po rdo rje'adzin// nyon mongs kun gyi rgya mchog no// 'bar ba grag po spyan yangs pas// gsung ni 'di skad bka' stsal to// lus dang ngag dang yid
22b5(rgyud): rnams ni// rnam par mi rtog mi dmigs pa// gang na'ang miganas mnyam pa nyid// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje sgom donas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rang bzhin gyis dag pa
22b6(rgyud): rol du phyin pa sngags kyi tshul rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhini gshegs pa de dag thams cad la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa ji spyod
22b7(rgyud): pa la sogs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rig pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du ma dang / thabs cig du sems can thams cad kyi don bya ba sa rol pa ston par mdzad de/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi
22b8(rgyud): khams mthas klas par 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga rnams kyis rol cing dges la yongs su spyod pa yod kyang / de dag sngags spyod pa la brtson pa rnams la/ kye ma 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
23a1(rgyud): spyod pa'i rgyas kyichos rdzogs par gyur tosnyas nas/ smyan ras kyis mi 'cho ste/ de bas na skyes bu ngam pa de dag la spyan ras rtsol ba'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung
23a2(rgyud): dang thugs dang / rdo rje'i sngags kyi bsang ba/ sngags thams cad kyi snying po kun tu skul bar byed pa zhes bya ba rab tu gsang ba zhes bya ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje
23a3(rgyud): kyi dam tshig la dmigs la rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi dam tshig la dmigs pa/ chos 'dzin pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi dam tshig la dmigs pa/ 'di nyid kyi sku
23a4(rgyud): gsung dang thugs rdo rje la sogs pa'i tshig gi lam nges par brjod/ pas sngags sdus pa 'di lta bu gsungs so// hUM/ oM A swA hA de nas 'di ni gsungs tsam gyis// sangs rgyas sras dang bcas
23a5(rgyud): pa kun// rab tu 'dar zhing rgyal bar 'gyur// rdo rje sems dpa rjes su dran// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos dam tshig 'di gsungs// na mkha'i dbying
23a6(rgyud): kying dbus gnas par/ bkod pa'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// de'i dbus nas yige hUM// rang gi gzugs su rab tu brtag/ rdo rje 'od zer cher 'bar ba// rnam par 'phro ba bsam par bya// sangs
23a7(rgyud): rgyas kyi ni sku gsung thugs// drangs par de yis rnam bsgoms na// de ma thag tu de 'gyur ba// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje 'dzin// rdo rje sems dpa' rgyal po che// kun gyi gtso bo dbang phyug samo// rang gi dkyil 'jor
23a8(rgyud): ra rdzog// bskyid par byed pa'i tshul du 'gyur// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// ming ba rdo rje bsdus pa yin// rang snapas skyes bur bsgoms nas ni// gnas pa ni rnams su sgomamanas ni/ thugs kyi dus
23b1(rgyud): zhal gsum lta bu'i sbyor ba yis// kha dog gsum du rab tu bsgom// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje dam tshig gis 'di skad ces bka' bstsal to// de la 'di ni rdo rje mchog gi gsang ba'o// snying kha'i dbus su phra ma
23b2(rgyud): dkyil 'khor rnams ni bsam par bya// yi ge mchog tu gyur pa'i tshig/ de'i dbus su bsam par bya// rdo rje chen po rtse lnga pa// rtag tu sbyor bas bsgom par bya// rdo rje skyo ba'i sbyor ba yis// rdo rje gsum rnams
23b3(rgyud): bsgom par bya// de yis snying khar gdab byas te// sgra rnams rab tu bskul bar bya// 'di ni rdo rje thams cad kyi// sangs rgyas byang chub rab sgrub pa'o// rdo rje pad mi rigs la sngogs// rdo rje kyo ba rnam
23b4(rgyud): bsgom zhing // snying kha ru ni skul bar bshad// 'di ni rol mo'i/ da'abyung ba ste// rdo rje yi ni tshul mchog 'di// zhag bdun bar du byas na ni// ye shes rdo rje can gyis gsang // sku dang gsung
23b5(rgyud): thugs 'grub par 'gyur// mchod brtsol pa dag rnam par gzigs yid ni 'jigs shing skrag gyur nas// yid la mgu zhing dga' 'gyur pa'i// dngos grub rgya chen ster bar 'gyur// sangs
23b6(rgyud): rgyas byang chub sems dpa' rnams// sngags kyi spyod pa'i mchog 'grub pas// rmongs pas mnga' bar byas na ni// de'i sdug ni der zad 'gyur// de nas rgyal ba rdo rje 'dzin// rdo rje gsum gyi ston pa mchog
23b7(rgyud): 'jig rten gsum mchog rdo rje gtsos// gsung ni 'di skad bka' stsal to// sngags kyi skyes bu ji snyed pa// rdo rje gsum gyi ye shes rdzogs// dbang po gnyis kyi sbyar ba yis// dngos po thams cad rtag par bya/ 
23b8(rgyud): 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// sngags kyi dam tshig bsgom pa'o// rig ma dbang phyug zhugs pa la// rdo rje'i sbyor ba rab bsgom zhing // chags la chags pas lta bar bya// 'di ni dam tshig 'khor lo'o// dorje
24a1(rgyud): rgyal ba rdo rje 'dzin// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi sras// thams cad dbang bskur sangs rgyas gtso// gsung ni 'di skad bka' bskul to// 'jig rten khams ni thams cad ni// bud med ji snyed yod pa kun
24a2(rgyud): phyag rgya che sdigs sbyor ba yis// de dag thams cad nye bar spyod// bye ba grangs med rdo rje 'dzin// sangs rgyas gnas ni der spro bya// bcom ldan 'das byang chub kyi dam tshig gis 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ 
24a3(rgyud): rdo rje gsum po mkho' 'dra ba'i// byang chub 'di yis thob par 'gyur// byang chub sems dpa' rgyal rgya mtsho// rdo rje sems dpa' che des thob// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsang dang
24a4(rgyud): thugs kyi gsang ba 'dus pa las/ de bzhin gshegs dpa thams cad kyi snying po skul ba zhes bya ba'i le'u ste/ bcu pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das sku dang gsung dang
24a5(rgyud): thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje skyes bu mchog ces bya ba'i ting / nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sdug
24a6(rgyud): rdo rje rig pa'i skyes bu'i le'u 'di gsungs so// rdo rje gsum yig sngags kyi mchog/ phyag rgya chen po rnam sdom pa// byang chub thams cad thob pa'i phyir// ye shes rdo rje dag gis bya// oM ni ye shes snying po
24a7(rgyud): rdo rje sku ni thob byed pa'o// A ni byang chub bdag med par// rdo rje gsung ni thob byed pa'o// hU~M ni sku gsung thugs yin te// rdo rje mi phyed gsum thob bo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
24a8(rgyud): sku dang / gsung dang thugs kyi bsngags kyi skyes bus de skad ces bka' stsal to// namakha' rdo rje dbus gnas par// dkyil 'khor rdo rje dbus gnas par// dkyil 'khor rdo rje kun skyes bsam// rdo rje sprin/ 
24b1(rgyud): ni 'phro skyed pa// de ru yi ge b+h+rUM bsam mo// de la 'di ni ye shes rdo rje'i snying po'o// b+h+rUM/ rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor rab gnas par// oM zhes bya ba rab tu bsgom// gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// yin
24b2(rgyud): a ni rnam par bsam// chos kyi 'khor lo dbus gnas par// yi ge hU~M ni rnam par bsgom// yi ge b+h+rUM ni gnas bsgoms te// rdo rje gsum byung bsgom par bya// bcom ldan 'das dam tshig gsang bas de skad
24b3(rgyud): ces bka' stsal to// snying po dus gsum sangs rgyas kyi// sku gsung thugs ni mnyes byed pa// oM ni sangs rgyas sku'i mchog/ oM a ni sangs rgyas gsung gi lam// a hUM ni ye shes thugs kyi dbyings/ 
24b4(rgyud): hUM byang chub tshul mchog 'di yin te// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// sangs rgyas byang chub rab sgrub pa// ye shes rdo rje'i sprul pa ste// sangs rgyas rgyu dang 'bras bu 'byung // 'di dag sangs rgyas
24b5(rgyud): skyes bu ste// sngags kyi rigs pa zhes kyang grags// rdo rje mi phyed gsum sgom pa'i// dam tshig dag gis sngoT/ par 'gyur// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / 
24b6(rgyud): thugs kyi dam tshig de kho na nyid kyi ye shes rdo rje byin gyis rlob pa'i dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// dben zhing rab tu nyams dga' bar// sbyor ba 'di ni kun rtsams nas// rdo rje'i sku dang gsung dang thugs// zla ba
24b7(rgyud): phyed kyis nges par 'gyur// gsal ba'i dkyis 'khor dam pa ni// namakha'i rdo rje'i dbus bsams te// rang gi sngags kyi dam tshig bskyed// yi ge a na sIng khar bzhag/ 'od zer lnga'i sprin chen po// rnam par
24b8(rgyud): snang mdzad mchog du bsgom// 'di yis sangs rgyas rnams kyi sku// rdo rje rnam snang rgya mtshor 'gyur// ye shes lnga ldan stan na ni// sangs rgyas sku ni 'dra ba'i mchod// rdo rje skal pa gsum du gnas// zla ba phyed
25a1(rgyud): kyis 'grub par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das sku rdo rje gsang bas de skad ces bka' stsal to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku rdo rje 'od zer bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// chos kyi rwa'o
25a2(rgyud): dram pa ni// nam mkha' rdo rje dbus su bsam// rang gi sngags kyi skyes bu bskyed// a ni lam la gyi lam bzhag ste// kha dog lnga'i pad ma mchog/ 'jig rten dbang mchog bsgom pa yis// dam
25a3(rgyud): tshig ye shes rdzogs byas te// tshig gi dam tshig lnga yis mchod// chos kyi chog gi lam gnas pa// rdo rje chos dang mtshungs par 'gyur// ye shes lnga ldan sten ni ni// rdo rje bskal pa gsum du gan
25a4(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gsung gsang bas// de skad bka'/ stsal to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung rdo rje'i dam tshig 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// rdo rje'i
25a5(rgyud): dkyil 'khor dam pa ni// nam mkha' rdo rje'i dbus su bsam rang sngags skyes bu rdzogs byas la// sems la yi ge hU~M gnas pa// dam tshig chen po de nyid ni// kha dog rnam lngar sgom par
25a6(rgyud): bya// rdo rje kun dang rgyal ba'i gnas// ye shes rdo rje dag gi cha// ston pa rdo rje'i thugs 'dra ba// ye shes yon tan rgya mtshor 'gyur// ye shes lnga ldan stenA na ni// rdo rje skal ba gsum du gnas// bcom
25a7(rgyud): ldan 'das thugs rdo rje'i thugs gsang bas 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi dam tshig rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// ye shes
25a8(rgyud): dkyil 'khor dbus su ni// rdo rje chen po sgom par bya// lus la rnam kun la khams dmigs nas// rdo rje ye shes na mkha' mnyam 'gyur lam// sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' yis// yang dang yang
25b1(rgyud): du mchod pa dang // skal pa gsum du yang dag gnas// sangs rgyas kyis kyang gzigs myi 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das na mkha' rdo rje dam tshig gis de skad ces bka' stsal to// sku dang gsung dang thugs rje
25b2(rgyud): rje mi snang ba 'byung ba bkod pa phreng ba bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// rdo rje dkyil 'khor dbus su ni// rang sngags skyes bur rab bsams na// snying khar rdo rje hriM zhes bya// bzhag ste 'od zer rnam par
25b3(rgyud): bsgom// haM// 'jam dpal dam tshig song spyod pa// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje can// sa bcu dag la gnas pa yi// byang chub sems dpa' de 'gyur// byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi dam tshig rdo rje zla
25b4(rgyud): ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// 'od zer 'bar ba'i mig ni dan mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus su bsam// mtshon tshogs rdo rje'i lus dag gis// rdo rje'i sku dang 'dra bar 'gyur// b+hI/ na mkha'i dam
25b5(rgyud): tshig gi bkod pa'i gnas zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// sangs rgyas mngon shes dam tshig mchog/ rdo rje 'chang dang 'dra bar 'gyur// 'di ni dngos grub thams cad kyi// sangs rgyas mngon shes
25b6(rgyud): mngon shes mchog sgrub pa'o// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dam pa bsam// rdo rje sems dpa' 'bar bsgoms la// ye shes oM ni bsam par bya// oM rdo rje'i da tshig
25b7(rgyud): gsum bsgoms pas// mi skyong rdo rje gsum 'drar 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje mi skyod pas/ de skad ces bka' bstsal to// mi skyod pa'i sku 'dra dang // gsung dang thugs mchog 'dra ba 'dzin// 'jig rten
25b8(rgyud): khams rnams thams cad du// mi skyod rdo rje mchod par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das mi skyod pa'i sku dang mnyam par mngon par 'byung ba'i dam tshig rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbusu ni/ 
27a1(rgyud): sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor 'od bzangs bsam// nam mkha' rdo rjer bsgoms la// rin chen oM ni bsam par bya// oM ni dam tshig rdo rje dam tshig gsum bsgoms pas// rdo rje gsum gyi dpal
27a2(rgyud): 'drar 'gyur// lus dang ngag sems rdo rje yis// dkon mchog dpal gyi 'od dang 'dra// de ni bdag med byang chub dang // ye shes gsang ba 'dra gnas 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo/ 
27a3(rgyud): rje dkon mchog dpal gyis de skad ces bka' stsal to// rin po che'i dam tshig longs spyod tshul zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus su ni// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dam pa bsam/ 
27a4(rgyud): 'jig rten dbang phyug ra bsgoms la// chos ni oM ni sgom par bya// oM// rdo rje dam tshig gsum bsgoms pas/ rdo rje gsum dpag med 'drar 'gyur// lus dang ngag sems rdo rje yis// 'od
27a5(rgyud): dpag med dang 'dra bar 'gyur// de ni sems can thams cad ni// theg chen lam ni 'byung bar 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das 'di dpag tu med pas/ de skad ces bka' stsal to// yon tan dpag
27a6(rgyud): tu myed pa rdo rje'i 'od kyi dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus su ni// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dran pa bsam// rdo rje ud pal la bsgoms la// dam tshig oM ni rab tu bsgom/ 
27a7(rgyud): oM/ rdo rje dam tshig gsum sgoms pas// rdo rje gdon mi za 'drar 'gyur// lus dang ngag sems rdo rje yis// rdo rje thogs med dang 'dra'i 'od// de ni dpal ldan ye shes mchod// sems can kun don
27a8(rgyud): 'byung bar 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gdon mi za bas de skad bka' bstsal to// rdo rje gdon mi za ba'i tshig 'od zer gyi ye shes kyi mchog 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi
27b1(rgyud): dbus su ni// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dam pa bsam// rdo rje snang mdzad 'dra ba'i 'od// de ni ye shes rdzogs byang chub// sku gsum mi phyed sgrub byed 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje rnam par snang
27b2(rgyud): mdzad kyis// de skad bka' stsal to// lus dang ngag dang yid mi dmigs// mngon par rdzogs byang chub par rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// rnam par dben pa'i ri bo dang // klu dang 'bab rgya rnams dang ni/ 
27b3(rgyud): dur gyi khrod la sogs par yang // bsam gtan bsdus pa 'di dag bsgom// mi skyod ye shes dag la sogs// rdo rje na mkha'i dkyil tu bsam// mngon shes lnga pa'i sbyor ba yis// sangs rgyas mchog
27b4(rgyud): gi gnas su sgom// bcom ldan 'das dam tshig chen po'i rdo rje'i mngon par mkhyen pas 'di skad ces bka' bstsal to// rdo rje chen po rtse lnga pa// 'bar ba lnga yis rnam par brgyan// gnas
27b5(rgyud): lnga dag tu sbyar ba yis// rdo rje mngon shes 'dra bar 'gyur// me stag mang po 'khrug pa yi// rang sngags 'khor/ lo bsgom par bya// rdo rje lnga po'i sbyor ba yis// rdo rje mngon shes 'dra ba
27b6(rgyud): 'gyur// rdo rje na mkha'i dkyil nyid du// 'khor lo sangs rgyas 'bar 'dra'i 'od// sangs rgyas 'jug pa rab bsgoms na// sangs rgyas gnas dang 'dra bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dbus
27b7(rgyud): gnas par// bdag gi lus la snang mdzad bzhag/ snying khar yi ge oM bsams la// sngags pa rnam par shes pa sgom// 'gog pa'i rdo rje sems nyid du// gang tshe de la skye 'gyur na// sangs rgyas kun gyi
27b8(rgyud): mchog 'dzin pa// yid bzhin dpal ldan lta bur 'gyur// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// rdo rje mi spyod rab tu bsgom// snying khar yi ge hUM sgoms nas// sems ni thig ler gyur pa bzhag/ 
28a1(rgyud): sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dbus par// tshe dpag med par rab tu bsgom// snying khar yi ge a bsams te// rdo rje thig ler gyur pa bzhag/ 'di de dam tshig mchog yin te// rdo rje mi phyed gsum
28a2(rgyud): sgom pa// 'gog pa'i dam tshig ye shes te// sangs rgyas dngos grub thob gyur pa'o// rdo rje na mkha'i dbyings gnas par// chos kyi 'khor lo sgom par bya// lus ngag sems la yi ge a// bsams nas de ni skam
28a3(rgyud): par gnas// rdo rje na mkha'i dbyings gnas par// rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor sgom par bya// lus ngag sems la yi ge hUM// bsams na de ni skal par gnas// rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor dbus sgom par// lus
28a4(rgyud): ngag sems la yi ge hUM// bsams na de ni skal par gnas// bcom dang ldan 'das rdo rje gsum gyi rtog pa'i dam tshig gis 'di ji skad ces bka' stsal to// sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje yi// rnal 'byor 'dir
28a5(rgyud): 'gyur phyin chad ni// klog gam yang sems kyang rung // de yang dan+ta/ tshig de rdo rje 'dzin 'drar 'gyur// de bzhin gshegs/ pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba// gsang ba 'dus
28a6(rgyud): pa las/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngags kyi dam tshig de kho na nyid rdo rje'i rigs pa'i skyes bu mchog gi le'u ste/ bcu cig pa'o// / de nas ston pa rdo rje 'dzin// bskyed pa
28a7(rgyud): ye shes mchog sgrub pa// dam tshig de nyid rdo rje gsum// rdo rje gsung gis bka' stsal pa// mkha' dang mnyam par mtshungs gyur pa// rnam par mi rtog ngo bo nyid// chos rnams rang bzhin dag pa la/ 
28a8(rgyud): rol mo 'di dag rab tu sgom// dgon pa chen po'i sa phyogs sam// me tog 'bras bu tshogs pas brgyan// ri bo dben pa'i sa phyogs su// dngos grub thams cad smras pa 'grub// maM// lus dang ngag seMs
28b1(rgyud): den sa// rje 'jam parab tu bsgos// smras dang gsems sa smos pas// rdorje las pa 'dra bar 'gyur// dpag cang brgya'i khyu l+h+waman+tu// de rje 'bang ba'i 'dodag gis// rgyu nunas kun gyis ldan
28b2(rgyud): pa yi// dag pa'i bdag nyid snang bar 'gyur// tshangs pa drag po la sogs smras// nam yang mthong bar mi nus so// rdo rje 'jam pa mchog gi mi snang ba zhes bya ba'i dring 'dzin to// rdo rje 'i phyed sum sas
28b3(rgyud): byung // gshang lci ra tshig snga rnams ni// lcags gsum las byung ldan byas te// khar bcug nas ni sdom par bya// sangs rgyas kun gyi mi byed pa'i// thugs ni de rur bsgom nas// rdo rje 'jam pa'i 'od 'phro hra/ 
28b4(rgyud): de ma thag tu de 'gyur ro// 'khor lo 'od 'phro mdangs mchogacan// rang gi sngags kyis rab bsgoms nas/ sangs rgyas thams cad bzhugs pa'i gnas// bsgoms na sangs rgyas
28b5(rgyud): 'dra bar 'gyur// ri rab sum bcu rtsa drug gis// rdul phran ji snyed yod pa rnams// rdo rje 'dzin dang 'dra ba kun/ de'i rjes su 'brang bar 'gyur// 'khor lo'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// 
28b6(rgyud): rdo rje chen po'i rang sngags kyis// dkyil 'khor dbus su rab bsgoms la// rdo rje kun gyi gnas yin par// bas mras na rdo rje 'dra bar 'gyur// ri rab sum bcu rtsa drug gi/ rdul phran ji snyed yod pa yi// de
28b7(rgyud): snyed kyi ni bud med rnams// yon tan can gyi gnas su 'gyur// drag po dag gis phyag byas bya// khams gsum rdo rje chen por 'gyur// dam tshig rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// pad ma chen po 'dab brgyad pa/ 
28b8(rgyud): rang sngags rdo rje bsams na su// chos rnams kun gyi gnas yin par// bsams ni chos dang 'dra bar 'gyur// ri rab sum bcu rtsa drug gi/ rdul phran ji snyed yod pa yi// sangs rgyas mchog mchod dkyil 'khor du// 
29a1(rgyud): dag pa'i bdag nyid 'jog par byed// pad+ma mo'i mnam nyid ces bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// ye shes lnga ldan rab bsten nas// bskul pa gsum gyi yun du gnas// phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas thams cad
29a2(rgyud): kyis// gsang ba gsum la bsnyen bkur byed// 'od zer lnga'i me tog dra ba'i 'od// rang gi sngags kyi ram gri bsgom// mig yangs lag na thogs na no// rdo rje ris sum rig 'dzin par 'gyur// khams gsum kun
29a3(rgyud): gyis rab mchod cing // tshangs dbang lnga min phyag byas pa// stong gsum na ni gcig pu pa// mi mchog gsang ba 'dzin par 'gyur// gang rnams 'dod dang bsam pa dag/ sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje 'dzin// rdo rje hUM
29a4(rgyud): la rab tu byung // de lta bu'i dngos grub ster// ras gri tha~Mng kyi dam pa zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// oM ni ri lu tsan ka'i// 'bru tsam du bsams na ni// dbus su rang gi lha'i gzugs// bas mas
29a5(rgyud): te khar bcug rnams bsgoms na// de'i de mA thag tu yang // byang chub ye shes 'od 'phror 'gyur// nyi ma shar ba'i 'od drang zhi 'dzam bu'i chu bo gser gyi mdog/ a ni ri lu tsa na ka'i// 'bru tshang
29a6(rgyud): tsam+ba du byasams na ni// dbus su rang gi lha'i gzugs// bsams te khar bcug rnams bsgoms nas// de ni de ma thag tu yang // byang chub ye shes 'od 'drar 'gyur// nyi ma shar ba'i 'dra 'dra zhing // 'dzam
29a7(rgyud): bu'i chu bo gser gyi mdog/ hU~M ni ra~M lu tsan+d+ra ka'i// 'bru tshad tsam du bsams na ni// dbus su rang gi lha'i gzugs// bsams te khar bcug rnams bsgoms na// 'khor mo'i rig pa// de ni de ma thag tu yang
29a8(rgyud): rdo rje sku dang 'dra bar 'gyur// na mkha' dbyings gsal ba'i dbus gnas par// rnam par snang mdzad rab tu bsgom// lag tu 'khor lo rab bsgoms nas// 'khor lo'i rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur// 'khor lo
29b1(rgyud): chen po rab bsgoms te// sangs rgyas sku ni rab sbyor zhing // ye shes sa 'dri ni rab sgrub pa// ye shes rdo rje dag gis bya// na mkha'i dbyings rdo rje'i dbus gnas par// ye shes mi skyod rab bsgoms te// lag tu
29b2(rgyud): rdo rje rab bsgoms nas// rdo rje rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur// rdo rje chen po'i rigs bsgoms te// rdo rje'i sku ni rab 'asbyor zhing // rdo rje mchog ni sgrub pa ni// ye shes rdo rje dag gi saM bya// na mkha' dbyings rin chen
29b3(rgyud): dbus gnas par// rin chen rdo rje rab tu bsgom// lag tu rin chen rab bsgoms na// rin chen rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur// rin po che'i rigs bsgoms na// rin chen sku ni rab 'byor zhing // rin chenani mchog ni
29b4(rgyud): sgrub pa ni// ye shes rdo rje dag gis bya// mkha' dbyings chos kyi dbus gnas par// tshe dpag med pa rab tu bsgom/ da lag tu pad mo rab bsgoms ni// pad mo'i rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur
29b5(rgyud): pe da mo'i rigs chen bsgoms nas su// chos kyi sku ni rab sbyor zhing // pad mo mchog ni sgrub pa ni// ye shes rdo rje dag gis bya// na mkha' dbyings rdo rje dbus gnas par// gdon mi za ba'i
29b6(rgyud): la ye shes bsgom// lag tu ral gri rab bsgoms nas// ral dri 'dzin pa rig par 'gyur// dam tshig chen po'i rigs bsgoms te// thogs med dam tshig rab sbyor zhing // dam tshig mchog 'di sgrub pa ni// 
29b7(rgyud): ye shes dag gis bya// rtse gsum ye shes lcags kyu mchog/ rdo rje'i khyad par gyis bsgrubs na// sku gsum thugs kyis sgrub pa yi// bsam gtan des ni 'grub par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das
29b8(rgyud): dam tshig chen po'i dngos grub rdo rjes de skad ces bka' stsal to// lam gyi bzhi mdo'am shing cig drung // mtshan ma cig dang zhi gnas su// rdo rje dgug pa'i khyad par gyis// bsgrub pa pos ni rtag tu bsgrub/ 
30a1(rgyud): sbyor gsum rdo rje can rnams kyi// sbyor gsum sngags kyi dam tshig bsam// sangs rgyas ye shes blo ldan gyis// sku gsung thugs kyi kyo ba dang // rlung gi dkyil 'khor mchog gnas pa// 
30a2(rgyud): sangs rgyas dgug pa dam pa yin// dam tshig las byung phyogs bcu pa// rdo rje bkug nas nye bar spyad// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dam tshig dgug pa'i cho ga'o// rnam par snang mdzad 'khor lo che// rdo rje
30a3(rgyud): padad+ma mo la sogs pas// rgyal nas lcags kyu bsams nas ni// dam tshig dgug mchog kyo bas bya// khams gsum dam tshig dgug pa'o// rnam pa mchog rnams kun ldan pa'i// sangs rgyas
30a4(rgyud): sku ni rab bsgoms la// lag tu sku dang gsung thugs kyi // / kyo ba la sngogs rab tu bsgom// 'di dag lta bu'i/ sbyor ba yis// de ni gnas las byed par 'gyur// rnam pa mchog rnams
30a5(rgyud): kun ldan pas// sangs rgyas rdo rje rab bsgoms na// rdo rje'i sbyor bas lce bsgoms na// rdo rje'i gsung dang 'dra bar 'gyur// rnam pa mchog rnams kun ldan pa'i// sangs rgyas skur ni rab
30a6(rgyud): bsgoms la// lag tu bsgrub bya bsems na ni// rdo rje dang ni 'dra bar 'gyur// gsang gsum dam tshig mchod pa'i mchog/ mchod pas mchod nas rab tu sgru ba// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// gas
30a7(rgyud): ba snying po bsdus pa yin// bcom ldan 'das gsang ba chen po'i dam tshig gis// 'di skad ces gsung so// she chen dam tshig mchog gis ni// rdo rje gsu'i mchog sgrub par bya// gshang lci dam tshig mchog
30a8(rgyud): gis ni// rig pa 'dzin pa'i gtso bor 'gyur// glang po sha'i dam tshig gis// mngon shes lnga dag thob par 'gyur// rta sha dag gis dam tshig gis// mi snang ba'i dam bdag por 'gyur// khyi sha dag gi dam tshig gri// 
30b1(rgyud): dngos grub thams cad 'grub par 'gyur// ba glang sha'i dam tshig gis// rdo rje dgug pa'i tshig tu 'gyur// shA rnams thams cad med na yang // thams cad bsams pas rnam par brtag/ rdo rje'i sbyor ba 'di byas na// 
30b2(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad byin gyis rlob// rnam pa mchog rnams kun ldan pa// sku gsung thugs ni rdo rje can// snying khar ye shes dam tshig can// dbu brgyan rdo rje mchog 'dzin pa// sangs rgyas thams cad snyems 'gyur/ 
30b3(rgyud): dam tshig dngos grub 'grub pa'i mchog/ dam tshig mchog gI rab tu 'jug/ thams cad ye shes rdo rjer gyur pa zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// lce'i dam tshig rdo rje mchog/ rdo rje can gyi hU~M bsgoms te// bdud rtsi
30b4(rgyud): yi sbyor ba yis// zos na rdo rje gsum thob 'gyur// a dang oM gyi dam tshig dang // rdo rje 'di ni rdo rje'i tshul mchog ste// 'di lta bu'i sbyor ba yis// rdo rje mi phyed 'dra bar 'gyur// rdo rje'i dam tshig 'dud rtsi'i phreng ba
30b5(rgyud): zhes bya ba'i tingange 'dzin to// rdo rje'i dam tshig gsum 'grub mchog/ sku gsum rdo rje can du 'gyur// phyogs bcu'i sems can thams cad kyi// nor bu yid bzhin rgya mtshor 'gyur// 'jig rten
30b6(rgyud): khams ni thams cad du// rdo rje'i bdag nyid snang bar byed// 'khor lo'i dam cige gsum 'grub mchog/ sangs rgyas su dang 'dra bar 'gyur// gang gi bye snyed thams cad du// grub pa kun tu rnam par spyod/ 
30b7(rgyud): dam tshig dam pa thams cad kyi// rig pa 'dzin pa'i gtso bor 'gyur// rdo rje'i sku ni rab bsgoms pas// dam tshig thams cad mchog tu 'grub// ji snang gyur pa thams cad du// stong khams dag ni snang bar byed// sangs
30b8(rgyud): rgyas kun las 'phrog pa dang // lha'i bu mo mchog la spyod// rdo rje gsum gyi gnas bzhugs la// rang lag skye ru ra bzhag yin// rdo rje mig gis mthong bar 'gyur// gang gi bye snyed rnams pa na// sgra grags pa ni ji snyed pa// 
31a1(rgyud): mngon shes rna ba thos pa ni// rna ba'i nang na 'khod pa bzhi// gang ga'i bye snyed zhing dag gi/ sems can kun gyi sems rnams ni// sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan ma yi// rol mo las byung sems rig 'gyur// 
31a2(rgyud): skal pa gang ga'i bye snyed du// 'khor ba dag na gnas pa ci// sngon gyi gnas kyi gtan tshigs rnams// zhag gsum lon pa bzhin du dran// gang ga'i bye ma lus kyi snyed// sangs rgyas sprin la sogs brgyan pas/ 
31a3(rgyud): bskal pa gang ga'i bye snyed du// rdo rje dam tshig rdzu 'phrul mchog gis 'gyengs// bcom ldan 'das dam tshig mngon par mkhyen pas/ de skad bka' stsal to// de la mngon par shes pa lnga ni/ rdo rje'i spyan dang / 
31a4(rgyud): rdo rje'i snyan dang / rgyu rdo rje'i gnas dang / rdo rje'i rdzu 'phrul lo// sangs rgyas mngon shes lnga don grub// sangs rgyas sku/ dang 'dra bar 'gyur// gang ga'i bye snyed grangs med pa'i// 'khor gyis
31a5(rgyud): yongasu bskor nas su// rdo rje'i sku dang gsung thugs kyis// 'jig rten gsum kun bgrod par 'gyur// snyen pa'i dam tshig sbyor ba dang // nye bar sgrub par 'byung ba dang // sgrub pa'i don gyi
31a6(rgyud): dam tshig dang // sgrub pa chen po dag dang bzhi// rdo rje'i bye brag shes byas la// de nas las rnams bsgrub par bya// sten pa'i dam tshig sbyor ba dang // nye bar sgrub par 'byung ba dang // bsgrub pa'i don gyi dam tshig dang / 
31a7(rgyud): bsgrub pa chen po dag dang bzhi// rdo rje'i bye brag shes byas la// de nas las rnams bsgrub par bya// snyen pa'i ting 'dzin rab sbyor ba// byang chub mchog ni sgom par bya// nye bar sgrub pa sgrub mchog la// rdo rje'i
31a8(rgyud): skye ba rnam par spyad// sngags kyi bdag po sgom pa yis// sgrub pa'i tshe la skul bar gsungs// bsgrub pa chen po byed pa'i tshe// rang sngags rdo rje can gyi gzugs// dbu brgyan la ni bdag po bsam// ye shes rdo rje
31b1(rgyud): 'grub par 'gyur// bsnyen pa'i ye shes bdud rtsi dag/ thams cad du ni rtag par bya// 'di ni sngags rnams thams cad kyi// sngags kyi de nyid don sgrub pa'o// dgon pa chen po'i sa phyogs dang // rab tu rnam par
31b2(rgyud): dben pa dang // ri bo nags 'dabs chu ngogs su// rtag tu dngos grub thob par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sgrub pa chen pos de skad bka' stsal to// yang na rdo rje bzhi dag gis// brtul zhugs bsnyen pa
31b3(rgyud): byasku gsum mnyam pa nyid gyur pa// sgoms nas dngos grub thob par 'gyur// dus bzhi dag du rab sbyor ba// blo dang ldan pas gnas sngar ni// ye shes rdo rje yi ge oM// bsgoms nas sdom pa yin par
31b4(rgyud): bshad// zhag bdun dang ni zla phyed dang // zla ba gcig zla ba phyed dang gnyis// rdo rje dam tshig bsgrubs na ni// dngos grub myur du thob par 'gyur// zhag grangs med brag rab skul ba// nga yi
31b5(rgyud): rgyas par rab tu brtag/ gsang ba mchog las byung ba la// zla ba phyed kyis 'grub par 'gyur// de la 'di ni nye bar/ sgrub pa'i sdom pa'i yul lo// sangs rgyas sku 'dzin dpal dang ldan// 
31b6(rgyud): rdo rje mi phyed gsum 'byed pa// byin gyis rlabs kyis gnas byas te// rdo rje sku dang ldan par bya// mi phyed rdo rje gsum bsgoms pas// phyogs bcur bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams// de la sku yis mtshan pa
31b7(rgyud): yid byin gyis rlabs kyis gnas mdzad do// de la 'di ni bsgrub pa'i sdom pa'i yul lo// chos kyi gsung lam dpal ldan pa// rdo rje mi phyed gsum byed pa// byin gyis rlabs kyis gnas byas te// rdo rje ga
31b8(rgyud): dang ldan par bya// rdo rje mi phyed gsum sgom pa// phyogs bcu'i bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams// de las gsum las byung ba yi// byin gyis rlabs kyis gnas mdzad do// de las 'di ni bsgrub pa'i chen pa/ 
32a1(rgyud): sdom pa'i yul lo// rdo rje'i thugs na bzhug pa'i sangs rgyas rnams// de la thugs las byung ba yi// byin gyis rlabs kyis gnas mdzad do// sangs rgyas rdo rje sems dpa' lam// yang na chos
32a2(rgyud): kyi sems dpa' 'ang rung // rmongs pas 'da' bar byed na ni// tshas par 'gas par gdon ni za// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa las/ 
32a3(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje sbyor ba'i dam tshig sgrub pa'i mchog bstan pa'i le'u ste// bcu gnyis pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan bde gshegs kun// ye shes rdo rje mchog
32a4(rgyud): 'dzin pa// sems can kun don yang dag 'byung // byang chub sems dpa' blo ldan gyis// thub pa don kun rdo rje can ston pa che la phyag 'tshal nas// de tshig de nyid mkhyen pa la// mchod rdo rje dbying
32a5(rgyud): 'di gsungs// e ma'i sangs rgyas tshul re bzang // e ma byang chub tshul gyi mchog/ e ma'o chos kyi zhi// e ma'o/ sngags kyi tshul re brtan// ma skyes pa'i chos rnams ni// ngo bo nyid kyis khyad
32a6(rgyud): par can// rnam par mi rtog yang dag las// ye shes 'byung ba rab tu bshad// yid 'ong sngags rnams kun smras pa// rdo rje bzlas pas ye shes che// sku gsum mi phyed dkyil 'khor dang // sangs rgyas ye
32a7(rgyud): shes thob 'gyur ba// rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms pa'i// rdo rje bzlas pa sbyor ba yis// sangs rgyas kun gyis byin gyis rlobs// rigs dang gsang sngags thams cad kyi// sku dang gsung dang thuT kyi mchog
32a8(rgyud): gsang sngags zlos pa de ring gsungs// ye shes rgya mtshogasan pa dang // sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje can// sangs rgyas dus gsum las byung rnams// rdo rje sngags ni rab sgoms pas// ye shes med pa/ 
32b1(rgyud): thob gyur pa// bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad du gsol// de nas ston pa rdo rje 'dzin// na mkha' rdo rje ye shes byung // skye med dam pa mchog gis gtses// rdo rje bzlas pa 'di gsungs pa// bsngags kyi don
32b2(rgyud): kun zlas pa ni// rdo rje mi phyed gsum gyi mtshan// rdo rje dbye ba gsum gyi mthar// bkod pa rdo rje gsum zhes bya// sku gsung thugs kyi gnas rnams su// spro ba rnam pa gsum dag bya// rdo rje bzlas pa 'di yI ni
32b3(rgyud): rdo rje gsum gyi thugs 'drar 'gyur// zhes kyang gsungs so// sangs rgyas kyi ni sku gsung thugs// bsgoms nas mchod pa'i mchod brtag pa// ye shes rdo rjes byas nas ni// rdo rje gsum gyi thugs 'drar
32b4(rgyud): 'gyur// sangs rgyas rnams kyi sku gsung thugs// bsams nas mchod pa'i mchod rtag pa// ye shes rdo rjes rab tu bya// 'di ni byang chub mchog thob pa'o// yang na dbye ba rnam pa gsum gyis
32b5(rgyud): so so dag tu spro bar bya// sku dang gsung thugs dbyer med/ bar// ye shes sems kyis yang dag spro// brjod nas rdo rje spro ba ni// rdzogs nas rab tu bsdu bar bya// 'di ni sangs rgyas
32b6(rgyud): spyan phye ba yi// sangs rgyas rnams ni kun gyi yin// sku'i rdo rje rdzogs byang chub// dngos dang dngos med rnam spyad pa// sangs rgyas sku zhes bya bar bshad// de ni sku'i bzlas par bshad// de ni sku'i
32b7(rgyud): bzlas par bshad// gsung gi dam tshig rdzogs byang chub// sgra dang sgra min rnam spyad pa// gsung gi rdo rje zhes bshad de// de ni gsung gau bzlas par bshad// thugs kyi dam tshig rdzogs byang chu
32b8(rgyud): gnas pa'i rdo rje rnam spyad pa// thugs kyi rdo rje zhes bshad de// 'di ni thugs kyi bzlas par bshad// don gyi rjes 'gro'i zlas pa yi// ngo bo nyid med bzang po yis// dus gsum sangs rgyas rnaM s+yang na/ 
33a1(rgyud): de ni rin chen bzlas par bshad// sangs rgyas zhing rnams thams cad du// sku'i sprin rnams spro ba dang // bzhud cing byin pa rdo rje'i don// de ni thogs med bzlas par bshad// khro bo'i dam tshig
33a2(rgyud): shes kyis// rang gi rdo rje dkyil 'khor grags// sngags kyi yi ge'i tshig thos pa// de ni khro bo'i bzlas par bshad// 'dod pa'i don gyis myos gyur pa// kun tu skyob cing phan par dga'// sems can gti mug
33a3(rgyud): gnas la 'jog/ de ni gti mug bzlas par bshad// 'dod chags rdo rje las byung tshig/ lus dang ngag sems la gnas pa'i// sems can 'dod chags mtshor gnas bzhag/ de ni 'dod chags zlas par bshad/ 
33a4(rgyud): zhe sdang rdo rje las byung sems// lus dang ngag sems la gnas/ pa'i// sems can zhe sdang gnas la bzhag/ de ni zhe sdang zlas par bshad// dam tshig de nyid rdo rje gsum// dbu ma dam tshig
33a5(rgyud): rdo rje can// de nyid dam tshig rdo rje yis// bzlas pa ma ning zhes bya'o// 'dod chags de nyid don sgom pa// rdo rje bdag po thams cad ni// sems can kun la pan 'dod pa'i// 'dod chags byang chub \u0f7f
33a6(rgyud): par mdzad// rin chen chen mo spyan la sngags// rtag tu 'dod pa'i don brtson pa// 'dod pa'i longs spyod dag gis ni// ji ltar 'dod pa ster na 'grub// gti mug dam tshig las byung ba// rig pa'i rgyal po rje
33a7(rgyud): rje can// ma ning dag la gri gnaso grub pa// dngos grub dam pa rab tu ster// khro bo ni sdang gnas las skyes// gsod la rtag tu brtson pa dag/ sgrub pa mchog gi chos can la// bsod pa'i don gyis 'gru
33a8(rgyud): par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das skyes bu chen po'i dam tshig gis// de skad ces bka' stsal to// ye shes 'khor lo can rnams kyi// 'khor lo snying gi dbus su sgom// gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus
