33b3(rgyud): chos kyi dkyil da'akhor dbus gnas par// pad mo sngags don sgom par bya// ral gri ye shes can rnams kyi// ral gri snying ka'i dbus su sgom// dam tshig dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// ral gri
33b4(rgyud): sngags don sgom par bya// dkyil 'khor kun gyi ngos rnams su sangs rgyas lnga rnams bsgom par bya// 'od zer lnga rnams bye brag gis// spros nas byang chub thob par 'gyur// sngags
33b5(rgyud): rnams thams cad skye ba ni// bye brag rnams gnyis su sgrags/ sku gsung rdo rje'i bye brag gis// spro ba dang ni bsku bar bya// lus kyi sku'i ngo bo nyid// sems kyi thugs kyi ngo bo nyid// ngag
33b6(rgyud): gis gsung gi ngo bo nyid// mchod nas mchod pa'i gnas su 'gyur// dkyil 'khor chen po'i 'khor lo yis// rdo rje lnga rnams bsgom par bya// dbus su bdag po bsams nas ni// sku gsung rdo rje rang
33b7(rgyud): gi gzugs// sngags rnams rdo rje gzugs dag gis// dkyil 'khor rnam pa bzhi dag du// kha dog rnam bzhir kun rtags la// snying khar sngags kyi don bsgoms na// rdo rje rnam pa bzhi'i las/ 
33b8(rgyud): bsam gtan rdo rje can dag byed// 'di ni sngags rnams thams cad kyi// gsang ba rab tu bzang po yin// zhi ba la ni spyan gyi tshul// rgyas pa la ni rdo rje pad mo spyan// dbang la rnam par snang mdzad gnas
34a1(rgyud): rdo rje khro bo mngon spyod la// 'di de thams cad kyi// gsang ba sku gsung las byung ba// sngags rnams kun ni sprul pa ste// bya ba'i rol mos mtshan pa'o// ma dang smra ba'i sems can dang // 
34a2(rgyud): rdo rje slob dpon smod pa dang // gdug pa'i sems can gzhan la'ang // rab tu skul ba 'di bya'o// bcom ldan 'das ye shes chen po'i 'khor lo rdo rjes de skad bka' stsal to// khams gsum gnas
34a3(rgyud): pa'i sems can rnams// sangs rgyas skur ni rnams sgoms la// dgra bo gsad par bsams nas su// de nas las rnams brtsam par bya// na mkha'i dkyi dbus gnas par// rdo rje rtse lnga kha bzhi pa
34a4(rgyud): rnam pa'i mchog rnams kun la ldan// rdo rje sems dpas/ rnam par sgom// dus gsum dam tshig las byung ba// sangs rgyas 'khor lo rnam bsgoms la// sangs rgyas 'khor lo stobs
34a5(rgyud): po che// lag pa g.yas pas 'di bya'o// phyogs bcu nas byung sems can rnams// sangs rgyas sku'i bye brag gi/ bsdus pa'i gong bu'i tshul gyis su// rang gi lus la de dag gzung / 
34a6(rgyud): sangs rgyas ye shes rdo rje can// slar yang spro bar rab tu bya// 'khro bos 'khrug pa'i khro bo rnams// mi sdug 'jigs su rung ba'i gzugs// mtshan che sna tshogs mchog 'dzin pa// gsad pa'i don gyi
34a7(rgyud): don sems pa// rdo rje sems dpa' rang nyid dam// gdug pa chen po gsod par byed// sangs rgyas sku gsum mchog rtsol ba// rdo rje gsum gyi dkyil 'khor gnas// nyi ma bdun du 'di byas na// sangs
34a8(rgyud): rgyas dngos grub ster bar 'gyur// rmongs pas grub pa mi ster na// 'chi bar 'dir mi gdon gyi za// rdo rje'i dam tshig ye shes kyi// bka'i 'khor lo zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// na mkha'i dbyings kyi
34b1(rgyud): dbus su ni// 'khor lo rdo rje 'bar bas brgyan// rnam pa'i mchog ni kun dang ldan// rnam par snang mdzad rab tu bsgom// dus gsum dam tshig las byed pa// rdo rje sems dpa' grags pa che/ 
34b2(rgyud): me stag 'phro ba can// de'i phyag na gnas par bsgom// phyogs bcu nas byung sems can rnams// rdo rje sku'i khyad par gyis// 'od zer tshul gyis bsdus nas ni// de dag bdag gi lus la gzud// sgo ba
34b3(rgyud): rdo rje thams cad kyi// ye shes mchog gi mnyes kyis bya// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje can// sangs rgyas thams cad bdag la gson// bdag ni dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzin// bka'i 'khor lo rab sgrub pa// gal te/ 
34b4(rgyud): dam tshig las 'das na// rdo rje rab tu 'bar ba yis// sku gsung las byung 'gas par gyis// zhig par 'gyur bar gdon mi za/ kra 'khor lo'i dam tshig ye shes rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ti nge 'dzin to// sangs rgyas
34b5(rgyud): dkyil 'khor rdo rje can// na mkha'i rdo rje'i dbus su bsam// gshin rje gshed kyi 'khor lo che// rang gi rdo rje yin/ par brtag/ dus gsum sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' rnams/ 
34b6(rgyud): sku gsum dkyil 'khor zhugs pa rnams// gshin rje gshed kyi mdog 'dra ba// slar spang sangs rgyas slo bar bya// dus gsum la bzhugs sems can dang // bdug sems can gyi dgra bo rnams// khros pas/ 
34b7(rgyud): thams cad gsad par bsgom// 'di ni rdo rje bka'i dkyil 'khor ro// dam tshig thams cad las byung ba sku gsung thugs kyi ye shes rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje 'am// rang sngags
34b8(rgyud): don gyi yon tan nam// yang na gtsug tor dam tshig gis// bka'i 'khor lo sbyor bar bya// sngags kun bsrung ye shes mchog/ rdo rje can gyis bya ba ste// 'di ni rdo rje thams cad kyi// byang chub bsrung ba'i don chen bya// 
35a1(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das rdo rjes de skad bka' stsal to// na mkha'i rdo rje dbus gnas par// chos kyi snang mdzad sku mchog las// bsams nas gdan du de rab brtag/ mkha'i dbyings sangs rgyas thams
35a2(rgyud): cad kyi// yongs su gang bar rnam par sgom// rang sngags yi ge'i gnas ye shes// thugs kyi rnam par sgom par bya// sangs rgyas rnams ni sems tsam du// bsgoms nas slar yang rab tu bsdu// thugs kyi
35a3(rgyud): rdo rjer byas pa'i phyir// sku gsung la na de dag gzung // rdo rje'i sngags rin po che rab tu snang bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// rnam pa'i mchog rnams kun ldan pa'i// rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu bsgom// sa
35a4(rgyud): rgyas rim par bkod nas ni// chu'i steng na bcug par bya// rkang pa mnyam bzhag skyo ba yis// skye bo'i steng du rkang pa bsgom// bcom ldan 'das ngo bo nyid dag pas de skad ces bka' stsal to// 
35a5(rgyud): rdo rje rgya mtsho rkang pas gnon pa zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// dbang chen dkyil 'khor bsgoms nas ni// dbus su khro bo rnams bzhag la// las kyi rdo rje'i rkang pa yis// de'i spyi bor gnon par som/ 
35a6(rgyud): mu stegs can pas kyi rgol pa thams cad kyi// 'khrul 'khor mnon pa zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// rdo rje gsum mchog khro ba'i tshul// ge sar ser po ri mdog 'dra ba// thams cad ri ba'i rgyal po ster// bas/ 
35a7(rgyud): nas spyi bor rab tu bsgom// sangs rgyas dpung yang gnod byed pa// mi dbang la ni dgos pa med// bcom ldan 'das de bzhini gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs las byung bas de skad
35a8(rgyud): bka' stsal to// dpung thams cad gnon pa zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// dgra bo skrag pa'i dam tshig gis// bsam gtan rab tu brtag pa 'di// sangs rgyas dag gis 'das na yang // 'gas par 'gyur
35b1(rgyud): gdon mi za// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gsum gyi dam tshig gis de skad gsungs// hU~M las phur bur bsam pa ni// rtse lnga pa'i tshad du ni// rdo rje phur bu'i de yis ni// snying khar 'dir ni rab sgoms na/ 
35b2(rgyud): khros pas sangs rgyas dpung dag kyang // 'jig par 'gyur bar gdon mi za// dgra ba rmongs par byed pa'i tingange 'dzin de// grong ngam yang na grong khyer ram/ ljongs dag tu ni rab sbyor ba// nad kun slong
35b3(rgyud): ba'i zhi ba yang // 'dis ni rtag tu sbyar bar bya// rdo rje rtse mo lnga pa ni// bar snang dag la rab tu sgom// grong ngam yang na grong khyer ram// skal pa sreg pa ltar bsams la// slar yang dka' ba yang rab
35b4(rgyud): tu 'gengs// spro ba dag kyang de nas kyang // rin chen yid bzhin nor bu'i 'od// chos kyi sprin ni bsgoms nas kyang // dbang ra skur ba ni yang dag bya// rdo rje'i bsam gtan 'di yis ni// dgang
35b5(rgyud): dka' ba yang rab tu 'gyengs// sbyin pa'i rdo rje sgom byed pa// yid bzhin nor bu dpal ldan 'gyur// sangs rgyas sprin dang chos chen dang // rdo rje sems dpa' der spro bya// skam
35b6(rgyud): pa gsum gyi yun gnas shing // sangs rgyas thams cad byin gyis rlob// 'di de sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// gsang ba'i sku ste skyon med pa'o// nad thams cad med par byed pa rdo rje 'byung ba zhes
35b7(rgyud): bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// bsam gtan las byung dam bcas pas// gnas gang du ni yang dag spyad// bsam gtan sbyor ba 'di yis ni// gnas na sangs rgyas byin gyis rlob// rdo rje bdud rtsi rgyal po// 
35b8(rgyud): rdo rje phur bu rab tu bsgom// me stag 'bar ba 'dra ba yis// phyogs bcu'i dkyil 'khor gdab par bya// zhes kyang gsungs so// 'gro ba 'dul ba zhi pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// zhi
37a1(rgyud): ba'i dkyil 'khor dam pa ni// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus su bsam// rnam par snang mdzad gzugs bsams nas// rang gi snying khar 'dod pa bzhag/ spyan la stsogs pa mchog rnams ni/ 
37a2(rgyud): mkha' dbyings yongs su gang bar bsgom// bsdus nas 'od kyi gong bu yis// nad pa la ni dbab par bya// ba spu'i bu ga nas sangs rgyas// sprin rnams rtul zhugs can gyis spro// sangs rgyas sprin
37a3(rgyud): rnams de'i tshe// de la dbang skur rab tu rtsol// nad pa rdo rje dam tshig des// skad cig gis ni dpal ldan 'gyur// sangs rgyas dam tshig bkod pa'i sprin zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor
37a4(rgyud): dbus su ni// dbang chen dkyil 'khor dam pa bsam// chos 'dzin pa'i gzugs bsams nas// snying khan 'dod pa bzhag par bya// na mkha'i dbyings nas nyams dga' bar/ 
37a5(rgyud): dkar mo zhes byas rab tu gang // 'od kyi grong bu bsdus nas ni// yid bzhin nor bu rin chen 'od// lus dang ngag dang sems gnas la// 'dod pa de la dbab par bya// ba spu'i bu grwa nas
37a6(rgyud): rin chen// sprin rnams tshul zhugs can gyis sgo// chos kyi sprin ni bsgoms su// dbang skur ba ni yang dag bya// rdo rje bsam gtan 'di yis ni// dgang dka' ba yang rab tu 'gongs// sbyin pa'i rdo rje
37a7(rgyud): sgrub pa bde// yid bzhin nor bu dpal ldan 'gyur// chos kyi sprin gyi dam tshig bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus su ni// rdo rje zla gam dkyil 'khor bsam// rdo rje rnam
37a8(rgyud): ma'i'i chos mchog gzugs// 'dod pa snying khar bzhag par bya// sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' yis// na mkha'i dkyil 'khor yongs su gang // 'od zer lnga yi sbyor ba yis// der ni gzi brjid
37b1(rgyud): \u0f7f// don cung // sa rgyas dun ci gas brtsod// lam la can 'dod dang d+hA// sa pan byed pa de lagyur// dbang gyur bani na/ dgyes pa'i ba/ 
37b2(rgyud): nyid de gsol bas// bsdus tsam skyed pa nyid kyis kyang // 'gro ba thams cad dbang du gyur// rin po che'i dam tshig gi sprin bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// namakha'i rdo rje srin po che// drag cing khrol
37b3(rgyud): rang tu ma dang // wa dang bya rod sna tshogs dang // bya nod khyi yis gang bar bsgom// mi'i dkyil 'khor la gnas par// dgra bo rnams ni rtag par bsgom// sangs rgyas kun la gnod pa byed// bsams
37b4(rgyud): nas rnal 'byor sbyar bar bya// mchod phyir sna tshogs thogs pas mnan// rgyul khrag dang klung la sogs// thams cad grangs par rnams sgoms te// bsgoms nas dgra rnams 'chi bar 'gyur/ 
37b5(rgyud): gal te de ltar rab bsgoms na// sangs rgyas rdo rje 'dzin pa yang // zla ba phyed ni tshun chad kyis// 'chi bar/ 'gyur bar gdon mi za// rdo rje dam tshig gi sprin bkod pa zhes bya ba
37b6(rgyud): ting 'dzin to// rnam par snang mdzad zhal gsum pa// ston kha'i 'dam bu'i mdog 'dra bsam// dkar po nag po rab tu dmar// thor tshug dbu brgyan dag gis brgyan// rdo rje can ni zhal gsum gsal
37b7(rgyud): nag po dmar po dkar po dmar po'i zhal// 'bar ba thor tshug dbu brgyan can// 'jig rten khams rnams 'khrugs med pa'o// 'dod chags can ni zhal gsum bsam// dmar po nag po dkar
37b8(rgyud): bo zhes// thor tshu gang dbu brgyan longs spyod can// bsgoms nas nges par 'grub par 'gyur// 'khor lo rdo rje pad mo che// g.yas pa'i phyag du rnam par bsgom// rdo rje phyag drug mtshon ma ni// bzang
38a1(rgyud): po sna tshogs snyams par bsgom// sems can kun sa phan gzhed ma// spyan ni zhas gsum dag tu bsam// dkar po nag po dkar po che// mdzes pa'i gzugs su rnam par bsgom/ 
38a2(rgyud): mkha' skyes spyan ni rgyal po che// zhal gsum du ni rtag par bsgom// nag dang dbar dang dkar ba'i tshul// mdzes pa'i gzugs su rnam par bsgom// chu skyes spyan ni rgyal mo che// zhal gsu du ni
38a3(rgyud): rnam par bsgom// dmar dang dkar dang gnag pa ste// kha dog mdzes par rnam par bsgom// rig ma rdo rje ud pal bsnams// zhas gsum rab tu gsal ba'i mdangs// ser dang nag dang dkar ba'i zhas// 
38a4(rgyud): sgoms na ye shes thob par 'gyur// khro bo chen po gshin rje gshed// zhal gsum drag po 'od bzang ba// rnon po 'jigs pa'ang 'jigs par byed// kha dog nag po rab tu sprom/ 
38a5(rgyud): gzhan gyis mi thub khro bo che// drag tu gzhad pa'i sgra yang 'jig/ zhal gsum 'od zer dmar po dag/ rab tu khro ba rnam par bsam// khro bo chen po rta mgrin ni// bskal pa'i me bzhin rab tu/ 
38a6(rgyud): 'bar// zhal gsum bdug pa'i zhabs kyis mnan// sbyor ba can gyis rtag tu bsgom// rdo rje mi phyed khro bo che// 'od zer khro ba rab tu 'khrug/ drag po 'khor lo 'bar ba 'dra// 'jigs pa dag kyang 'jin
38a7(rgyud): par byed// 'dod pa'i ye shes khro ba che// zhal gsum pa ni 'jigs par byed// phyag bzhi 'jigs par byed pa'i mchog/ tra ki rgyal po rab tu bsgom// stobs po che ni rdo rje che// 'jig rten gsum ni
38a8(rgyud): mun sol ba// 'dug pa thams cad 'joms par byed// napa gsung por ni rtag par bsngos// khro'i chen po byug sngon can// khams gsum dag ni 'jigs par byed// nas gsum rdo rje gsum sa
38b1(rgyud): 'bar ba rnon po can du sgom// rdo rje mi g.yo rab tu sgom// rdo rje las byung mi g.yo// zhi ba ral gri zhags pa bsnams// brtul zhugs can gyis zhal gsum bsgom// gtsug gtor chen po yi ge gcig/ 
38b2(rgyud): 'od zer dag ni kun tu 'phro// zhal gsum 'bar ba 'khor lo can// bsam gtan dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// gnod mdzes ye shes mchog 'dzin pa// 'jigs pa'i rgya mtsho yang dag byed// zhal
38b3(rgyud): gsum rab bzang sgom par bya// bsam gtan 'bar ba 'od bzang bsgom par bya// gzi brjid 'od bzang gtsug tor rgyal// gang gzhan sngags kyi 'khor lo can// de tshig long spyod 'di rnams kyis// so so /

38b5(rgyud): par// gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor dam pa bsam// sangasargyas gzugs ni rab sgoms la// rnam par snang mdzad rnam par bsam// gsal zhing zhi la zla ba bzhin// 'od zer
38b6(rgyud): sna tshogs 'dra ba'i 'od// me long lta bur yang dag byung // khams gsum dag gi dkyil 'khor du// brgyan rnams kun gyis brgyan pa dag/ bsams na de yis byang chub thob// bsam gtan rdo rje rab
38b7(rgyud): sgom pa// 'di yis sangs rgyas che ba'i bdag/ 'jig rten thams cad dbang byed pa// tshe 'di nyid kyis thob par 'gyur// rnam par snang mdzad kyi dam tshig 'byung ba mdzes pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting

52b2(rgyud): ni las rnams thams cad kyi// 'jigs shing shin tu mi bzad yin// dgra bo'i gzugs brnyan byas nas ni// gshang gci dag ni chos thams cad// zhog can// tsher ma'i me la khros nas sreg/ sangs rgyas
52b3(rgyud): ngag kyang nges par 'jig/ chu bo'i 'gram gnyis sa yis kyang // dgra bo'i gzugs byas nas ni// til 'bru tsam gyis yan lag kun// dug las byung ba'i tsher ma yis// skul ba'i tshig dang bcas pa dag/ 
52b4(rgyud): sangs rgyas dag kyang nges par 'jig/ skye tshe lan tsha 'bru mar dang // dug dang da ru ra dag ni// sangs rgyas thams cad gsad pa la// 'di dag mchog tu gyur par gshad// sol lus gsher
52b5(rgyud): ba'i gos dag ni// gyon te sems ni khros nas su// rkang pas ling ka mnan nas su// srin po'i khyer bar gdon mi za// rus phye khrag dang dug rnams kyis// gzugs brnyan rab tu byas nas
52b6(rgyud): ni/ rdo rje sems dpa' grag po yang // myur ba dag du khyer bar 'gyur// skye tshe bshad gci sbyar ba yis// ling g.yongs su gang bar ni// blugs na rkang pas rab gnan nas// tsha ba chen pos btab par 'gyur
52b7(rgyud): de la 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig chen po khro bo'i snying po'o// na ma sa man ta ka ya waka tsing badz+ra nam/ oM hu lu hu lu/ tiSh+Tha triSh+Tha/ b+han d+ha b+han d+hu/ ha na ha na/ da nga dra ha/ gardza gardza

53a1(rgyud): \u0f7f/ 'di ni gsod pa'i mchog yin no// rdo rje sems dpa' khro bo ni// rnam par bzad pa 'jigs 'jigs lnga// sta ri tho ba phyag na bsnams// bsams nas bsam gtan rab tu bya// de la 'di ni
53a2(rgyud): drab po chen po'i khro bo'i dam tshig go// mkha' dbyings thams cad sangs rgyas kyis// yongs su gang bar rab du sgom// gdug par de yis gsad par ni// bsams nas de sa thag tu 'chi// sangs rgyas byang
53a3(rgyud): sems dpa' yis// yongs su gang bar bsgoms nas ni// bdug pa'i sems pas gsad na ni// rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid kyang 'chi// sangs rgyas gnod byed dgra rnams la// skrag cing 'jigs par bkrugs
53a4(rgyud): ba ni// sngags mkhan gyis ni mdun bsams nas// 'chi bar ra 'gyur bar gdon mi za// sprin po khro bo sna tshogs dpa// gtum zhing khro ba mi zad pa// der ni skrag par byar bsams na/ 
53a5(rgyud): rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid kyang 'chi// 'ug pa khAng bya rgod dang // mnu ring ba dang wa rnams ni// de yis zos par bsas na ni// sangs rgyas dag kyang nges par 'jig/ sbrul nag rab tu khro
53a6(rgyud): ba ni// 'jigs pa drag kyang 'jigs par byed// dug gi mchog gi dam tshig 'di// dpral bar bsams nas khyad 'phags pa'i// sbrul des zos par bsam na ni// sangs rgyas dag kyang nges par
53a7(rgyud): 'jig/ phyogs bcu'i sems can thams cad la// yams sam gnod pa byed pa rnams// 'jig pa nges par 'bebs pa'i mchog/ 'di ni skul ba'i mchog yin no// tho ba rab tu drag po yis/ 
53a8(rgyud): brtul shugs can gyis snying khar brdeg/ rdo rje 'dzin pa'i bka' bzhin du// dgra'i srog ni med par 'gyur// rdo rje sta re la sogs pas// gshag cing brngub par bsams nas ni// sku gsum gyi ni
53b1(rgyud): mchog sbyin pa// rdo rje sems dpa' drag lo 'ang 'chi// bsrung ba la sogs rnams dang ni// lha rnams dang ni phur bus btab// 'di ni bsod par byed pa'i mchog/ dam tshig shin tu 'da' dka'o// 
53b2(rgyud): rdo rje phung pos ci tsam du// sems can dkyil gnas pa la// gsad bdag nyid gtogs bsams na ni// mnyes par 'gyur te gzhan du min// ston po sangs rgyas rdo rje 'dzin// rdo rje chos dang rdo rje can// 
53b3(rgyud): rdo rje thugs kyi bka' bzhin du// bsam gtan sbyor bas 'chi bar 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das khro bo'i chen po'i dam tshig khro bos de skad bka' stsal to// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// thams cad
53b4(rgyud): na mkha' thub chen po// thams cad dbang skur rdzogs sangs rgyas// ye shes rdo rjes bka' stsal pa// e dma'o ngo bo nyid kyis dag/ rdo rje theg pa bla na med// me skyes pa'i chos
53b5(rgyud): rnams las// rgyal ba rnams kyis skye bar ston// de la 'di ni las phran tshogs kyi rdo rje gsang ba'o// sbrul ni mi sdug 'jigs byed pa// nag po 'bar ba 'khrug cing g.yo// lce
53b6(rgyud): gnyis mche ba'i phreng can ni// rdo kyus dag gam sol bas bri// de la 'di ni khro bo skul ba'i snying po'o// khaM// mi zad par ni gyur pa'i dug/ rdo rje dbus na 'dug par bsam// sreg pa me'i kha dog
53b7(rgyud): bzhin// sgom na 'gul bur gdon mi za// de la 'di ni dug thams cad 'byin pa'i snying po'o// d+hI// rnam pa sna tshogs las byang dug/ khams gsum na ni gnas pa kun// de yis khyer bar sgoms na
53b8(rgyud): ni 'bab par gyur pa rnam par bsam// de ni de ma thag tu yang // mi zad dug ni mtshor mi 'gyur// reg ma thag tu skye bo kun// 'jig par 'di la the tsom med// sdig pa sbal pa la sogs dang da
54a1(rgyud): sbrul rnams sna tshogs pa dag kyang // sbyor ba 'byung ba'i mtshan nyid kyis// cho ga bzhin du rab tu bya// de la 'di ni dug thams cad 'pho ba'i snying po'o// oM/ lnga ba rdo rje'i dug la sogs// gzha
54a2(rgyud): yang mi zad pa'i dug/ na mkha'i rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor du// bsams nas ye shes rdo rje 'dren// bcom ldan 'das dug gi dam tshig chen po'i rdo rje'i de skad ces bka' stsal to// de la 'di ni dug bso ba'i dam
54a3(rgyud): tshig rdo rje'i snying po'o// hUM// rdo rje chen po'i snying po 'di// kha dog dkar por rnam par bsam// 'od kyis sprin ni shin tu 'bar// zla ba'i 'od zer bzhin du bsil// gnas bzhi dag du sbyor ba yis// de ma thag
54a4(rgyud): du 'byung bar 'gyur// lan gsum legs par bsgoms na ni// skyugs pa dag du rnams bsams na// na mkha'i khams kun gang ba yang // de ma thag tu dug med byed// ces de skad bka'

54a6(rgyud): pa tsam gyis med par 'gyur// pad ma chen po 'dab ma brgyad// zla ba bzhin du dri med pa// de'i dbus na 'dug bsam pa// 'od zer lnga ni rdzogs pa'o// sdud pa dang ni dam tshig gnag/ skul ba de ni dkar
54a7(rgyud): po 'dra// bsam gtan gnas ni gsang ba 'di// ye shes dri med gsang chen yin// de la 'di ni phyi nang gi nad thams cad gso ba'i rdo rje'i snying po'i sngags kyi yi ge'i tshig rnams so// dzi na dzi ka/ a ro li ka/

54b1(rgyud): rang gi lus ngag sems gnas las// byung ba dag tu rnam par bsam// 'khor lo 'am ni gur nang du// bsgoms na rdo rje'i go 'phang gnas// lus dang ngag sems dam tshig rnams// des ni phye mar brlag
54b2(rgyud): par bsgom// de nas rtsams te rdzogs sangs dang // byang chub sems dpa' grags chen rnams// byin rlabs go 'phang dam pa dag/ dges pa'i spyan ni rab tu rtsol// zhes de skad bka' stsal to// rang lus
54b3(rgyud): ngag sems rdo rje la// sangs rgyas sprin dag rnam par bsam// rdo rje rgyal po sprin chen po// nad las thar bar bsgom par bya// phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas thams cad dang // blo ldan byang chub sems dpa'
54b4(rgyud): dag/ de la khros par bsams na ni// 'chi bar byed par dam pa yin/ bsam gtan sbyor ba 'di dag gis// las skyesasu yang gang grags pa// brgya rtsa brgya zlas sbyor ba yis// nyi ma bdun

59a4(rgyud): 'on kyang rdo rje can bdag nyid// gshang gci'i khu ba'i dam tshig gis// mchod na dngos grub thob par 'gyur// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// dam tshig shin tu 'da' dka' ba'o// 
59a5(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung gi dkyil 'khor ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa kun nas sprin gyi tshogs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms pa

59a7(rgyud): gnas su 'gyur// sku gsung thugs kyi gsang las byung // 'di ni dra bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i gnas ye shes gsang ba yin te/ rab tu gsang ba'o// de nas
59a8(rgyud): phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi 'khor lo zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi sku dang / thugs rdo rje'i gsang ba 'di nyid kyi sku dang / 
59b1(rgyud): gsung dang thugs rje rje las byung ngo // de la 'di ni rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi sngags kyi snying po'i mdo'i yi ge'i tshig rnams so// oM a hUM/ rdo rje'i thig ni gdab pa dang // mtshon rtsi la sogs dgye bdag/ sngags kyi
59b2(rgyud): sems dpa'as mi bya'o// byas na byang chub rnyed par dka'// de bas dam tshig tshul shes pas// sngags kyis lnga rnams phab nas su// byin gyis brlabs kyi gnas sgoms la// dkyil 'khor rnams ni rnam
59b3(rgyud): bar rtag/ rgyal chen rnam par snang mdzad dang // yang ni spyan ni dbab par bya// sku'i dkyil 'khor gnas yid 'ong // rdo rje'i sku'i yon tan tho ba// rdo rje chos ni rgyal po che// rang gi chos mas dbab par bya/ 
59b4(rgyud): 'di ni sngags rnams thams cad kyi// gsang ba rab tu rtog pa yin// rdo rje sems dpa' rgyal po che// ma ma ki yang dbab par bya/ 'di ni sngags rnams thams cad du// gsang ba rmad du byung ba'o// de ltar
59b5(rgyud): byas na byin rlobs cing // yid la dbang ba nyid gshegs te// kye rab tu dgyes par gyur nas ni// gsang ba dag gis/ mchog kyang rtsol// 'di skad kyang ni gsungs so zhes// sngags kyi seMs
59b6(rgyud): dpas bya ba ni// rdo rje gsang ba rmad po che// khro bo'i rgyal pos su/ gnas ni// sangs rgyas thams cad mchod par bya// rdo rje dri snod gsum dag gis// dam tshig mchod pa dus gsum la// rdo rje gsum
59b7(rgyud): gyi sbyor bas bya// sngags kyi dngos grub thob par byed// 'di skad kyang gsungs so// sngags rnams cad nyid la yang // rmad du byung ba'i gtor ma bya// gshang gci sha dang 'bru mar dang // sems las byung ba'i
59b8(rgyud): tan tan dang // khu ba dag gis sngags rnams kun// tshim par gyur par kun tu bshad// 'di ni dam tshig yin te// sangs rgyas byang chub rdzogs byed pa'o// thig btab pa'i cho ga 'di// bdag nyid gang tshe spyod
60a1(rgyud): rnam par snang mdzad snyoms nas su// rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu sgom// yang na rdo rje mi cher grags// slob ma rdo rje 'od po che// sangs rgyas kun gyis nges pa yi// las kyi go 'phang sgom par bya/ 
60a2(rgyud): sangs rgyas rgyal chen lnga rnams ni// rdo rje'i thig skud dag la dgod// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// gsang ba rmad du byung ba'o// rnam pa nyi shu rtsa lngar ni// mtshon rtsi dag kyang rnam par sgom// 'di ni sangs
60a3(rgyud): rgyas thams cad kyi// gsang ba byang chub dam pa yin// sngags rnams thams cad nyid la yang // rdo rje hU~M ni bsgom par bya// sku dang gsung dang dam tshig mchog/ gnas lnga dag tu sgom par bya// de ltar rtag
60a4(rgyud): tu byas nas ni// rdo rje mi phyed gsum las skyes// rdo rje sems dpa' blo ldan pa// 'jigs shing skrag nas byin rA ba mdzad// rdo rje bum pa bzhag pa ni// sngags rgyud bdag pos shre
60a5(rgyud): bya ste// rdo rje sems dpa'i ting 'dzin gnas// brtan pa'i blo ni rtag par bya// dngos grub kun gyi 'bras 'dod pa'i// sAg+sa shes pas ni sbyin sreg bya// gshang gci 'bru mar sha la sogs/ 
60a6(rgyud): sbyin sreg du ni 'bul bar bya// rdo rje mi phyed gsum dag la// rdo rje gang ba'i sbyin sreg dbul// dbus su rang gi lha'i gzugs// bsams nas zhal du dbab par bya// 'di skad kyang gsungs so// dbang
60a7(rgyud): gnyis kyi dam tshig gis// sbyin sreg brgya rtsa brgyad du bya// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// dam tshig shin tu 'da' dka' ba'o// rnam snang mdzad kyi sbyor ba yis// slob ma rdo rje gsum las byung // a ni
60a8(rgyud): lus dang ngag sems la// bsgoms nas rdo rje bzung bar bya// rgyal chen rdo rje sems dpa' dang // grags chen rnam par snang mdzad dang // sku gsung thugs kyi dam tshig tu// byin gyis rlabs ni rab tu rtsol// des
60b1(rgyud): 'di ni dkyil 'khor chen por 'jug pa'i rdo rje'i dam tshig go// a khaM bi ra hU~M/ 'di ni dam tshig thams cad kyi lus dang / ngag dang sems rdo rje'i snying po'o// de la 'di ni rdo rje chen po dbang skur ba'i// gsang ba'i ye shes
60b2(rgyud): gsang ba'o// sangs rgyas kun gyi na mkha'i khams// yongs su gang bar rab tu sgom// rdo rje'i rigs ni 'dzin pa yis// sil snyan dri'i sprin rnams so// 'di skad kyang gsungs so// rdo rje sku gsum sngags kyis
60b3(rgyud): yungs dkar dag gis gdab par bya// de la de'i tshe na ni// bdag nyid dbang skur rab tu rtsol// rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyis// yang na sangs rgyas sgom par bya// bum pa'i dam tshig mchog rnams kyis
60b4(rgyud): bzung bar mkhas pa dag gis sgom// rdo rje rnam par snang mdzad bsam/ slob ma rtag tu blo ldan la// lus dang ngag sems rdo rje can/ sngags shes pas ni dgod par bya// de la dbang skur ba thams cad
60b5(rgyud): kyi gsang ba slob dpon thams cad kyi rdo rje'i dam tshig du smra bar bya'o// sangs rgyas rnams ni thams cad kyi// rdo rje gsang ba/ gsum las byung // khams gsum dag gis phyag byas pa// rdo rje/ 
60b6(rgyud): 'i dbang skur chen po sbyin// de la 'di ni slob ma thams cad kyi rdo rje chen po'i gsol ba bya ba'i cho ga gsang ba'o// byang chub rdo rje sangs rgyas la// mchod min ji ltar rtsal ba ltar// bdag kyang rab tu gral
60b7(rgyud): sgral ba'i phyir// na mkha'i rdo rje deng bdag rtsol// de tshe de la dbang skur ba// rab tu dges nas rtsol bar mdzad// lha'i gzugs kyi sbyor ba yis// snying khar bdag po bzhag par bya// rdo rje slob ma blo ldan
60b8(rgyud): li// sngags kyi yi ge'i tshig na byin la// dkyil 'khor dag ni snyan par bya// sangs rgyas kun gyis gsungs pa yi// dam tshig gsang ba sgrags par bya// khyod kyis srog chags gsang bar bya// brdzun gyi tshi kyi
61a1(rgyud): smra bar bya// ma byin par yang khyod kyis blang // bud med dag kyang sten par bya// rdo rje lam ni 'di dag gis// sems can thams cad skul bar bya// 'di skad ces gsungs te/ 'di ni sangs
61a2(rgyud): rgyas thams cad kyi// dam tshig mchog tu rtag pa'o// sngags kyi bskul ba sgrags pa yis// de la sngags kyang sbyin par bya// sngags kyi rgyal po'i ting 'dzin dang // gsang ba sbyin pa rtsam par bya// khub
61a3(rgyud): 'am gshang ba'ang rung // cho ga bzhin du bsngags nas ni// rdo rje blos ni bza' bar bya// 'o na dngos grub rnyed mo dka'// rnam pa 'di bzhi gsang chen te// rdo rje can ni kun gyi gsang // sngags kyi 'khor
61a4(rgyud): lo bud med gzugs// sems can don spyod phyir gnas so// de la 'di ni rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi sngags mnyes par bya ba gsang ba'o// glang po'i sha dang rta'i she// sha chen
61a5(rgyud): dag kyang bza' bya zhing // sngags rnams kun la dbul bar bya// de ltar byas na mgon po mnyes// nyin re rdo rje'i slob ma la// mkhas pas dkyil 'khor bstan par bya// gshang lci
61a6(rgyud): sha'i bza' ba dang // rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig dag gis// sngags rnams kun gyi yi ge oM// bsgoms na de ma thag tu 'bar// bcom ldan 'das sngags kyi rig pa'i skyes bu chen pos de skad bka' stsas te

62a1(rgyud): cad kyi gsang ba'i rdo rje gsang ba'o// rdo rje sems dpa'i ye shes che// de bzhin gsung gi rdo rje 'dzin// rdo rje sku'i bkod pa ches// mngag gzhugs pa dag rtag tu skul// de la 'di ni rdo rje ye shre/

64a7(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rig pa'i rdul zhugs kyi dam tshig gi de kho na nyid kyi rdo rjes de skad ces bka' stsal to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang
64a8(rgyud): ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa las/ don grub thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor mngon par byang chub pa zhes bya ba'i le'u ste// bcu drug pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
64b1(rgyud): thams cad yang 'dus nas// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa pa la gsol ba btab pa/ mi skyod rdo rje ye shes che// rdo rje dbyings ni mkhas
64b2(rgyud): chen po// rdo rje gsum mchog dkyil 'khor gsum// rdo rje dbyings la phyag 'tshal lo// rnam par snang mdzad dag pa che// rdo rje zhi ba dga' chen po// rang bzhi no 'od gsal mchog gi mchog/ ston pa rdo
64b3(rgyud): rje phyag 'tshal lo// rin chen rgyal po rab tu zab// rdo rje na mkha' dri ma med// rang bzhin dag pa gos pa med// rdo rje sku la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje dpag med rgyal po che// mi rtog na mkha' rdo rje 'dzin/ 
64b4(rgyud): 'dod chags pha rol phyin pa rnyes// rdo rje gsung la phyag 'tshal lo// don yod rdo rje rdzogs sangs rgyas// bsam pa thams cad rdzogs mdzad pa// dag pa ngo bo nyid las byung // rdo rje sems dpa' phyag
64b5(rgyud): 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas kun gyis skul ba yi// bstod tshig bzhi pa 'di nyid kyis// rdo rje long slod bstod na ni// de yang sangs rgyas 'dra bar 'gyur// de nas ston pa rdo rje 'dzin// sangs rgyas kun
64b6(rgyud): la rjes rtse ba// rdo rje gsang ba'i gsung dag la// rdo rje gsung ni bka' stsal to// e ma'o sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// chos kyi dbyings ni yi ge che// rang bzhin 'od gsal yongs su dag/ na mkha'i dbyings
64b7(rgyud): bzhin dri ma med// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sku'i rdo rje 'dzin// tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung // sangs rgyas
64b8(rgyud): rgya mtsho yos// dam tshig bzhi ni bsrung bar bya// sha chen dag tu bza' bar bya// 'di ni dam tshig mchog yin no// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa'i bdag pos// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsung
66a1(rgyud): gi rdo rje'i dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las byung ngo // dam tshig bzhi po bsrung bar bya// gsung gi yi ge thig le che// gshang gci dag ni rtag tu bzar// 'di ni gsang ba
66a2(rgyud): rmad 'byung ba'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung // rdo rje sems dpa' rdzu 'phrul che// dam tshig bzhi po bsrung
66a3(rgyud): bya// khrag dang khu ba sbyar ba dag/ rtul zhugs brtan pas rtag tu bza'// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje yi sa// dam tshig 'di ni rmad po che// sangs rgyas kun gyi rtag pa 'di// rdo rje 'dzin gyis bsrung
66a4(rgyud): ba 'dis// gang zhig dam tshig 'di bsrung ba// rdo rje sems dpa' 'od po ni// de'i sku gsung thugs rtogs pa// de ma thag tu sangs rgyas 'gyur// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin ga
66a5(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi bdag pos// rang sangs rgyas kyi don gyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyungango // de'i lus ni ston pa ni// rdo rje sku la rab tu gnas// sems
66a6(rgyud): can gzud pa'i ngang tshul te// dam tshig mchog tu rtag pa'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos// nyan thos kyi bslab pa'i dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs
66a7(rgyud): rdo rje las phyung ngo // dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam// byed pa ye shes spangs pa rnams// dman pa mos pa thams cad kyi// dam tshig 'di ni rmang po che// sangs rgyas kun gyi rtag pa 'di// de nas phyag na
66a8(rgyud): rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos tshangs pa'i dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang sku gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyungango // gti mug lam gyi las gang rnams// byed pa 'jigs shing rtag pa 'ami sdug
66b1(rgyud): sangs rgyas byang chub ston pa ste// sku'i rdo rje nyid du 'gyur// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ drag po'i dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // 
66b2(rgyud): khams gsum dag na gnas pa yi// bud med rdo rje las byung rnams// sna tshogs dngos po spyan nas ni// dam tshig mchog tu rmad 'byung ba'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
66b3(rgyud): bdag pos khyab 'jug gi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // sems can las byung ji snyed pa// dbyer med sku gsung las 'das pa// rdo rje mkha' dbyings bdag nyid
66b4(rgyud): kyang // bsam gtan rdo rjes gsad par bya// skye'i rdo rje tshangs par 'gyur// gsung gi rdo rje dbang phyug che// thugs kyi rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// de nyid khyab 'jug rdzu 'phrul che// de nas phyag na rdo rje de
66b5(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ gnod sbyin mo thams cad kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung / dang thugs rdo rje las phyungango // khrag dang sha ni za ba dang // rtag tu gzhan
66b6(rgyud): gyi bud med spyod// dam tshig dka' 'di rnams kyis// rdo rje chen po mnyes par byed// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ klu'i rgyal po thams cad kyi dam tshig 'di
66b7(rgyud): nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung // 'o ma 'thung ba phru ma can// dri dag 'dod dang dri la 'bad// dam tshig 'di ni bsgrub par bya// gzhan du nges par nyon mongs 'gyur// de nas phyag na
66b8(rgyud): rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ lha ma yin gyi bu mo'i dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las phyung // khro zhing nga rgyal gsod pas gnon// spos dang me tog
67a1(rgyud): spyod las skyes// rdo rjes 'og dam tshig ste// gdus dga' dzi 'jigs pa'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ srin mo rnams kyi dam tshig 'di nyid
67a2(rgyud): kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las byung // thod rus bdug pa'i 'bru mar dang // zhag gis rab tu dga' bar 'gyur// 'byung po kun gyi dam tshig ste// dag byed 'dri ni don chen byed// de nas
67a3(rgyud): phyagan rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos// rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma thams cad kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // gshang gci dang ni khrag dag za// mang
67a4(rgyud): lo sogs pa'ang rtag tu 'byung // rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyor pa yis// gnas kyi mtshan nyid kyis gsang byung// ngo bo nyid kyis kun 'byung ba// khams gsum dag na rnam par spyod/ 
67a5(rgyud): sems can kun la phan 'dod pa// dam tshig ma lus spyang par bya// khams gsum pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i tshigarjes su 'breng ba zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// de nas phyag na rdo rje de
67a6(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ lus kyi dngos grub kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung // lus kyi rnam gsum thams cad ni// rdo rje las ni byung bar bya// sems
67a7(rgyud): can khams ni thams cad du// rtag par sangs rgyas sku byed pa'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag bos/ ngag gi dngos grub 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las byung// 
67a8(rgyud): tshig gi lam gnas ma lus par// khams gsum dri med dkyil 'khor to// tshig gi dngos grub yid 'ong 'di// dam tshig shin tu 'da' dka' ba'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams
67b1(rgyud): cad kyi bdag pos sems can rdo rje'i dam tshig dngos grub 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las byungo // yid kyi rdo rje'i rang bzhin kun// rdo rje brtan pa 'dzin pas bsgom// rdo rje mi phyed gsum ldan gyis/ 
67b2(rgyud): dam tshig bshad pa 'di yin no// bcom ldan 'das kun tu mdzes dga' rdo rje sems dpas de skad ces bka' stsal to// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ sngags thams
67b3(rgyud): cad kyi rdo rje'i snying po dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung // sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dang // rang rgyal nyan thos de bzhin te// sku gsung thugs kyi sbyor ba ni// phyag
67b4(rgyud): 'tshal na ni ma rung 'gyur// de nas yang phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje 'iri bsam gtan
67b5(rgyud): gyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyu/ kun tu rdo rje sems dpa' yi// sku dang gsung thugs kyi dkyil 'khor la// bsam gtan rdo rje gsum sbyor bas// sngags zlos
67b6(rgyud): pas ni bsam gtan bya// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos// sngags sgrub pa'i dam tshig dang sdom pa nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las byung // mdor na sems can
67b7(rgyud): khams rnams ni// bsam gtan rdo rjes skul bar bya// rdo rje gsum gyis phyag 'tshal mchog/ dam tshig rdo rje las byung ba'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ bsnyen pa
67b8(rgyud): sgrub pa dang / dam tshig rab tu rtag pa'o// nye bar sgrub pa dang // bsgrub pa chen po'i sgom pa nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung // rdo rje gshang gcis na mkha'i dbyings// yongs su gang bar rnam pa bsta
69a1(rgyud): dus gsum rdo rje dag la dbus// dam tshig rab tu brtag pa'o// de nas phyag rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ rdo rje mi snang ba thams cad kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung
69a2(rgyud): dang thugs rdo rje las byung // dus bzhir ji ltar mchog bzhin du// rdo rje mo ni nyin re spyad// yang ni rdzas ni rtag tu dbrog/ dam tshig rdo rje rdzogs byed pa'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
69a3(rgyud): kyi bdag pos/ na mkha'i rigs 'dzin gyi dam tshig nyid kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje ni// dbu brgyan dag la bsam gtan bsam// rdo rje gsung gi dam tshig ste/ 
69a4(rgyud): khros pa rnams kyis mi thub bo// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ sngags 'chang las kyang dang po pa rnams kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las
69a5(rgyud): byung ngo // sku'i rdo rje'i kha zas pa// phyi rol rdo rje 'dzin pa dang / mdo don chog bya bas// rtag par rdo rje chos su bya// bcom/ ldan 'das ngo bo nyid mnyam pa nyid la rnam par dgongs dag pa rdo rjes de
69a6(rgyud): skad ces bka' stsal to// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad kyi sku dang thugs kyi snying po rdo rje mnyam pa nyid la rnam par dgongs nas/ cang mi gsu
69a7(rgyud): bar gyur to// de nas brjod du med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing ri rab kyi rdul rab tu phra ba dang // mnyam pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la phyag 'tshal// 
69a8(rgyud): nas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po 'di ci'i slad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi nang na cang mi
69b1(rgyud): gsung bar bzhugs// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang
69b2(rgyud): thugs kyi bdag po 'di sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rdo rje'i ngo bo nyid dmigs su med pa'i yi ge'i tshig la ngo bo nyid med pa'i yi ge'i tshig brjod nas/ cang mi gsung bar bzhugs so// rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa
69b3(rgyud): thams cad kyi bdag po 'di sems dpa' na 'di snyam du gyur to// sku mi 'gyur pa ma skyes pa// gsung dang thugs kyang mtshan ma med// nam mkha' rdo rje tog las phyung // log par bzung bas zin pa yin// de nas
69b4(rgyud): 'jam dpal la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' chen po rnams kyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa de la 'di skad gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad gsung rdo rje'i tshig la phyin ci log
69b5(rgyud): kun 'byung bas mi rtag tu gsol// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ de/ bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po 'di na// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i dbyings kyi ngo bo nyid spyong bar 'gyur ba'i
69b6(rgyud): rjes su 'gro'o// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ tshangs pa la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' chen po mngon par shes pa chen po'i ye shes thob pa rnams chos thams cad kyi mtshan nyid ngo bo nyid mi shes nas/ 'di snyam
69b7(rgyud): ngadu rnam par rtog te/ rdo rje'i bdag nyid 'di de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi rdo rje'i de kho na nyid yongs su shes na/ gsang ba'i yi ge rnams 'chad dam snyam du sems pa yang mchis so// de nas
69b8(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad bka' stsal to// / byang chub sems dpa' khyed rnams lta ci smos te/ nged de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
70a1(rgyud): sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i gsang ba mi 'gyur mo rnyed pa/ sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi byang chub mi shes so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ skye ba med pa rdo rje'i mngon par byang chub pa'i ngo bo nyid med pa mi 'gyur
70a2(rgyud): ba las byung ba'o// rigs kyi bu sems can chen po'i khongs su gtogs pa'i sems can ji snyed yod pa de dag thams cad byang chub la gnas pa sangs rgyas rdo rje'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sems can de dag ni
70a3(rgyud): sku gsum rdo rje'i chos nyid kyi phyir sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i ye shes thob pa'o// phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i ye shes thob pa'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de
70a4(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i bdag pos/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad gsungaso// rang bzhin dag
70a5(rgyud): cing bdag med la// chos kyi cha dbyings ni gnas med pa// rtog pa rdo rje las byung ba// smra ba med pa smra ba yin// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis/ bcom
70a6(rgyud): ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa phyag na rdo rje chen po la phyag 'tshal nas/ 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku/ dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje dngos grub yang dag
70a7(rgyud): par ji ltar 'jug/ gang na gnas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po rdo rje 'dzin pas gsungs pa/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dngos grub thams cad dang / thams
70a8(rgyud): cad mkhyen pa dang / khams gsum ji snyed pa dag rang gi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rgyud kyi rdo rje la gnas so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis slar gsungs pa/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
70b1(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje dngos grub thams cad gang na gnas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos gsungs pa/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams
70b2(rgyud): cad kyi bdag po ye shes rdo rje'i sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi dngos grub dang / khams gsum pa thams cad kyi nam mkha' la gnas so// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsungs pa/ 
70b3(rgyud): nam mkha' gang na gnas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos gsungs pa gang na yang ma yin no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag ngo mtsharu du gyur/ rmad du gyur nas/ e ma'o rdo rje e ma'o rdo rje
70b4(rgyud): e ma'o rdo rje yis bshad pa// gang du lus dang ngag sems med/ dre ru gzugs ni rnam par sgom// de nas ston pa rdo rje 'dzin// sangs rgyas kun gyis phyag byas nas// rdo rje gsum mchog mchog chen
70b5(rgyud): mchog/ rdo rje gsum gyis dbang phyug mchog/ rig pa'i skyes bu bsgom pa yi// dngos grub gyis ni bshad par mdzad// mkha' dbyings rdo rje'i dbus gnas par// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor
70b6(rgyud): sgom par bya// rdo rje'i sku ni rab sgoms na// spyi bor rdo rje rab tu bsgom// zhal gsum sku gsum las byung ba// rnam par 'phro bar bsam par bya// rdo rje 'khor lo 'dzin bsams na// byang chub myur du thob
70b7(rgyud): par 'gyur// thams cad rigs kyi bye brag gis// gsang ba 'di ni rnam par bsam// gzhan tu rnam par bsgoms na ni// de dag dngos grub mi 'gyur la// bcom ldan 'das rig pa'i skyes bu rdo rje gsang bas// 
70b8(rgyud): de skad bka' stsal to// dbyings gyur pa ni rgyal mo che// mnyes par byed pa rnams bsams na// rdo rje sku ni gsum gyi mtshan// khyu mchog des ni mnyes par 'gyur// gang zhig 'di dag sgom pa yi// bya
71a1(rgyud): chub sems dpa' grags chen rnams// zhag bdun gyi ni gzi chen pa'i// sku gsum dngos grub thob par 'gyur// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje bsdus pa'i
71a2(rgyud): gsang ba 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // sku gsung thugs kyi dam tshig ni// phyag rgya chen po'i don rtag pa// cho ga bzhin du kun bsgoms na// skad cig gis ni sangs rgyas
71a3(rgyud): thob// de nas phyag ni rdo rjes bsgrub pa po thams cad kyi lus dang ngag dang / sems gsang ba nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las byung // g.yong byang chub mchog 'dod na// lag pa'i phyag rgya
71a4(rgyud): bcing ngo // sngags rnams kun gyi dam tshig 'di// rgyal ba kun gyi mi 'da'o// de nas phyag ni rdo rjes sangs rgyas kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyungango // gshang
71a5(rgyud): khu ba khrag rnams ni// smad pa dag du yod mi bya// cho ga bzhin du rtag tu bza'// sngags 'dri rdo rje gsum byung / yin// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rjes/ gsung
71a6(rgyud): rdo rje'i dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // khams gsum dag gi lam mchog na// bud med ji snyed yod pa rnam thams cad chog bzhin du spyan// gsung gi rdo rjes mi snad
71a7(rgyud): de nas yang phyag na rdo rjes/ thugs kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las byung // rdo rje gsum la mkhas pa mi// dam tshig ji snyed yod bkun// rdo rje gsum gyi dam tshig gis// mthu
71a8(rgyud): zhing tshim pa dag tu bya// thugs kyi rdo rje ma snad do// bcom ldan 'das dam tshig chen po gsum gyi dam tshig gis de skad bka' stsal to// de nas yang phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
71b1(rgyud): bdag pos/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba'i rdo rje nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung // mdor na phung po lnga rnams ni// sangs rgyas lngar ni rab tu skyugs// rdo rje skye mched
71b2(rgyud): nyid dag kyang // byang chub sems dpa'i dkyil 'khor mchog/ de nas phyag na rdo rjes khams/ gsum gyi 'khor lo 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung // sa ni spyan ma ni zhes bya ba yin/ 
71b3(rgyud): chu'i khams ni ma ma~M ki/ dkar dang sgrol ma zhes bya ba// me dang rlung du rab tu bsgrags// mkha' dbyings rdo rje'i dam tshig ni// rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid yin// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams
71b4(rgyud): cad kyi gnas kyi dbang phyug rdo rje sems dpa' chen pos de skad bka' stsal to// de nas bcom ldan 'das sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mnyam pa

108a5(rgyud): de kho na nyid kyis// rlung gi de nyid rnal 'byor mchog/ yang dag rtsom pa byas pa gsal// kha zas byed pa bzhin du ni// thog mar sa ni yongs su sbyangs// de stong sgrogs dang bral byas la// gnas ni leH
108a6(rgyud): par dag par bya// khang bzangs shin tu nyams dga' ba// blo ldan ji ltar 'dod par bya// de bzhin rnal 'byor pas shes bya// rlung gi de nyid rnam par sgom// snga ma bzhin du mnyam bzhag nas// srog dang rtsol ba'i

108b1(rgyud): shig le zhes ni bshad// yang dag de nyid gsang ba yang // sna rtser yungs kar de yang ni// rgyu dang gzhan rnams gsungs pa yi// sna rtser yungs dkar de yang ni// srog dang rtsol ba'i rtags pas ste// srog rtsol ba la gnas
108b2(rgyud): pa dang // 'od lnga sangs rgyas lnga ru sgom// steng gi sna las nges 'byung ba// g.yon dang g.yas dang gnyi ka dang // dal ba rgyu dang rnam bzhir 'gyur// nang gi dus ni yin par bshad// lkog ma snying kha lte ba dang // gsang

109b1(rgyud): ma sbyor skyes// mi phyed dbye ba rnam par sbyangs// de'i ngo bo de nyid de// rang nyid tshor ba rig pa'o// pha rol gzhan gyi spyod yul min// dpe' bral mtshon par dka' ba dang // rang gi blos yang dag gnas// rang rig pa zhes

110a1(rgyud): ye shes ni ba nyid// gnyis med mchog tu gse ru'o// de dag bde ba rtogs pa yi// de dang bral ba'i bde chen po// gang phyir mchog tu dga' ba'i dus// nyan thos ye shes ma brjod do// de'i mtha' bral gnas pa ni

263a1(rgyud): de nas 'kha 'gro'i tshogs de dag thams ca rab tu dga' nas// ca co'i sgra yang dag par 'byin cing // dbyangs chen po brjod par gyur to// kye ma rdo rje sems dpa'i// rdo rje shin tu dgyes chen tha/ 
263a2(rgyud): kye ma'o sna tshogs thabs ni bde byed che// sna tshogs ye shes bde ba che// kye ma'o kun tu bzang po mi// dgra ba'i ye shes bde 'byed che// gang 'de'i phyir ni ma rig pa'o// pad mol ni gnas par 'dzod//
